CHAPTER I. GENERAL PROVISIONS 

§1. Purpose 

The  purpose  of  these  Enforcement  Rules  is  to  stipulate  the  matters  necessary  for  the 
enforcement  of  the  KONEX  Market  Listing  Regulation  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  “the 
Regulation”).   

§2. Definitions 

(1) The  terms  used  in  these  Enforcement  Rules  shall  have  the  same  meanings  given  to 

them in the Regulation.   

(2) The term “those professional investors specified in the Enforcement Rules” in [§2(6)] of 
the Regulation shall refer to the investors falling under each of the following subparagraphs:     

1.  Professional  investors  under  Article  10(1)1  and  2  of  the  Enforcement  Decree  of  the 
Financial Investment Services and Capital Markets Act (hereinafter referred to as “the 
Enforcement Decree of the Act”); 

2. Professional investors under Article 10(2)1 through 10 and 13 through 16the Enforcement 
Decree of the Act. Provided that a trust company, discretionary investment company and 
investment  advisory  company  shall  be  excluded  from  among  the  entities  under  Article 
10(2)8of the Enforcement Decree of the Act; 

3. Professional investors under Article 10(3)3 and 10 through 13 of the Enforcement Decree 
of the Act; and 

4. As the professional investors equivalent to those noted in paragraphs(1) through (3), those 
professional investors for whom the Exchange deems it appropriate to exclude the shares 
held by them when calculating the number of shares owned by the largest shareholder in 
consideration of the nature of the investors concerned and the purpose of their shareholding, 
etc.   

(3)  “Technology  evaluation  grade  set  forth  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  [§2(14)]  of  the 
Regulation shall be grade BB or higher pursuant to [Annex 4]. In such case, the technology 
evaluation  grade  shall  refer  to  the  evaluation  of  technological  prowess,  etc.  as  separately 
determined by the Exchange and the calculation of the grade according to the superiority or 
inferiority of technology, etc.: [June 30, 2016] (Amended on December 29, 2016) 

CHAPTER II. DESIGNATED ADVISOR 

1 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
§3. Appointment Contract for Designated Advisor 

(1) “Cases that are specified in the Enforcement Rules” in the proviso to the part except each 
subparagraph of [§4(2)] of the Regulation shall refer to the cases where a designated advisor 
intends to submit the liquidity provision quotation pursuant to [§22(4)] of the Enforcement 
Rules of the KONEX Market Business Regulation. [June 19, 2017] (Amended on April 17, 
2019; April 28, 2022) 

1.  [Deleted on April 28, 2022] 
2.   

      2. [Deleted on April 28, 2022] 

(2) “Matters prescribed by the Enforcement Rules” in the latter part of [§4(3)] of the Regulation 
shall refer to matters in each of following matters: (Amended on June 19, 2017) 

      1.Matters concerning the pledge of compliance with financial laws and the business-related 

regulations of the Exchange between the corporation and the designated advisor:   

      2.Matters related to the officer and the employee in charge of affairs, the scope of work, 
and contact procedures and means, etc. between the corporation and the designated advisor.; 

      3.Matters  concerning  confidentiality  of  information  received  from  the  other  party  and 

prohibition of improper use of the information; 

      4.Matters  concerning  rights  and  obligations  of  the  corporation  and  designated  advisor 

concerned; 

      5.Matters  concerning  notification  of  changes,  etc.  in  business  and  organization  of  the 

corporation and designated advisors concerned; 

      6.  Matters  concerning  fees  paid  in  return  for  the  performance  of  duties  of  a  designated 

advisor; 

      7.Matters concerning the termination of the appointment contract for the designated advisor; 

and 

      8. Other matters that the Exchange deems necessary. 

(3) A KONEX-listing applicant and a KONEX-listed corporation shall enter the appointment 
contract for the designated advisor with one (1) designated advisor. 

§4. [Deleted on June 11, 2015]

§5. [Deleted on June 11, 2015] 

§6. [Deleted on June 11, 2015] 

§7. [Deleted on June 11, 2015] 

§8. Measures against Designated Advisor 

(1) [Deleted on June 11, 2015] 

(2)“Cases  stipulated  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  [§7(3)1]of  the  Regulation  shall  refer  to 
[§28(1)2,34,  14-2,  14-3]  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  “the  cause  for  designation  of  an 
administrative issue in the KOSDAQ Market”)in the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation and 
[§38(1)2,  4,  4-2,  5  (limited  to  a  case  where  the  cause  for  dissolution  is  a  adjudication  of 
bankruptcy),  10,  11  and  §38(2)3  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  “the  cause  for  delisting  in  the 
KOSDAQ  Market]  of  the  same  Regulation.  [June  26,  2014]  (Amended  on  June  11,  2015; 
January 31, 2018; April 17, 2019) 

(3)“Cases  stipulated  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  [§7(3)2]  of  the  Regulation  shall  refer 
to[§28(1)1,  5,  6  (limited  to  a  case  where  the  cause  for  dissolution  is  a  adjudication  of 
bankruptcy), 7, 9 (limited to a case where the appointment contract for the designated advisor 
is  terminated  after  the  occurrence  of  causes  stated  in  [§28(1)7,  10  and  [§28(2)2]  of  the 
Regulation.[June 26, 2014] (Amended on January 31, 2018) 

(4)In order to  deliberate on whether to  take  an  action within 15 days  (if there is  a need for 
additional investigation, the period may be extended within 15 days) for the date on which any 
of cases stipulated in each subparagraph of [§7(3)] of the Regulation is identified, The KONEX 
Market  Listing  and  Disclosure  Committee  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  “the  Committee”) 
pursuant  to  [§36]  of  the  Regulation  shall  hold  a  meeting,  and  a  decision  shall  be  made  on 
whether  to  take  the  action  within  3  days  from  the  date  of  deliberation.[June  26,  2014] 
(Amended on June 19, 2019; April 17, 2019; June 10, 2020) 

(5)The period of suspension of qualifications as a designated advisor pursuant to[§7(3)] of the 
Regulation shall be as follows: [June 26, 2014] (Amended on June 11, 2015; April 17, 2019) 

      1.In the case of falling under a cause for the designation as an administrative issue in the 

KOSDAQ Market: within six (6) months; 

      2.In the case of falling under a cause for the delisting in the KOSDAQ Market: within one 

(1) year; 

      3.In the case of falling under [§7(3)2] of the Regulation: within six (6) months; and 

      4.In the case of falling under [§7(3)3] of the Regulation: within three (3) months. 

3 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(6) Where the Exchange takes an action to suspend the qualification of a designated advisor 
pursuant  to  [§7(3)1]  of the  Regulation  because  a  KOSDAQ-listed  corporation  falls  under  a 
cause for delisting, it shall take measure excluding the period of suspension of qualification as 
a designated advisor due to the designation as an administrative issue in the KOSDAQ Market. 
[June 26, 2014] (Amended on June 11, 2015) 

(7)In the case of multiple cases falling under each subparagraph of [§7(3)] of the Regulation, 
the Exchange may take measures by adding up the period by case of suspension of qualification 
as  a  designated  advisor  to  the  designated  advisor.  In  this  case,  the  period  of  suspension  of 
qualification for a designated advisor shall not exceed one (1) year. [June 26, 2014] (Amended 
on June 11, 2015) 

§8-2. Procedures for Appeal against Measures Taken to Designated Advisor 

(1) The designated  advisors shall submit the following documents when  filing an objection 
pursuant to [§7(2)] of the Regulations: 

      1. A statement of reasons for objecting to the Exchange’s decision and documentation of 

evidence thereof; and 

      2.Other documents that the Exchange deems necessary in relation to the objection. 

(2)  If  an  objection is  filed pursuant  to  paragraph  (1), the Exchange shall hold  a  Committee 
meeting  and  grant  the  representative  of  the  designated  advisor  concerned  an  opportunity  to 
state his/her opinion. (Amended on March 11, 2020) 

(3)The  Exchange  shall  determine  whether  to  take  an  action  against  the  designated  advisor 
within three (3) days from the date of deliberation by the Committee pursuant to paragraph (2). 

[June 26, 2014] 

§9. Checking of Duty Performance of Designated Advisor, etc. 

(1)Designated  advisors  shall  prepare  appropriate  standards  and  procedures  for  checking 
compliance with the obligations, etc. prescribed in [§8] of the Regulation and regularly check 
the operation status. 

(2) In case of falling under any of following subparagraphs, it shall be deemed a “conflict of 
interest” stated in [§8(3)] of the Regulation. [June 26, 2014] (Amended on June 27, 2016) 

      1.Where  the  designated  advisor  holds  5/100  or  more  of  the  stocks,  etc.  of  the  issuing 

corporation; or 

      2.Where the designated advisor and the stakeholder of the designated advisor together hold 

4 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
10/100 or more of the stocks, etc. of the issuing corporation 

(3) When calculating the ownership ratio of stocks, etc. under each subparagraph of paragraph 
(2), stocks, etc. acquired after the conclusion of  an appointment contract  for the designated 
advisor  stated  in  [§4(3)]  of  the  Regulation  are  excluded,  and,  when  an  association  or 
organization,  falling  under  any  of  following  subparagraphs  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  “the 
relevant association, etc. in this paragraph),in which the designated advisor or the stakeholder 
of the designated advisor invested holds stocks, etc. issued by the corporation, it is deemed that 
the concerned designated advisor or the stakeholder of the designated advisor owns stocks, etc. 
that  correspond  to  his/her  investment  ratio  in  the  relevant  association,  etc.  among  the 
corporation-issued stocks, etc. held by the relevant association, etc.:[June 27, 2016] (Amended 
on December 29, 2016; June 19, 2019; March 8,2021) 

1.  Venture investment association stated in Article 2/11 of the Act on Facilitating 

Venture Investment; 

2.  New technology venture investment association stated in the Specialized Credit 

Finance Business Act; 

3.  [Deleted on March 9, 2021] 

4.  Privately-placed fund stated in Article 9(19) of the Act 

§10. Report by Designated Advisor, etc. 

“When  there  is  other  resolution,  decision  or  occurrence  of  a  matter  prescribed  in  the 
Enforcement  Rules”  in  [§9/9]  of  the  Regulation  shall  refer  to  any  of  the  following  cases:   
(Amended on June 11, 2015) 

1.  [Deleted on June 11, 205] 

2.  When a resolution for a merger is made or such decision is made; and 

3.  When there is other resolution, decision or fact affecting the performance of duties of 

the designated advisory. 

§11.[Deleted on June 11, 2015] 

CHAPTER III. LISTING 

5 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
§12. Documents to Be Submitted for Initial Listing, etc. 

(1) “Application for initial listing (hereinafter referred to as “the initial listing application”) 
stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in [§12(2)] of the Regulation shall refer to [Listing Form 
No. 3] and “report for listing eligibility (hereinafter referred to as “the listing eligibility report”) 
prepared by the designated advisor in charge shall refer to [Listing Form No. 4]. (Amended on 
December 29, 2016) 

(2)  “Corporations  prescribed  by  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  the  part  other  than  each 
subparagraph of [§12(2)2] of the Regulation shall refer to those that have been audited on the 
financial statements (limited to the case where the auditor’s opinion is “unqualified”) for the 
latest fiscal year by an accounting firm that is not an auditor pursuant to [§3] of the Regulation. 
[April 17, 2019] 

(3) “Documents specified in the Enforcement Rules” in [§12(2)5] of the Regulation shall refer 
to the document under each of the following subparagraphs: (Amended on November 13, 2013; 
October 2, 2014; September 10, 2019; December 10, 2021) 

1. Articles of Incorporation;   

2. [Deleted on October 2, 2014];   

3. The minutes of the board of directors meeting that approved the listing decision;   

4.  The certificate of issuance and registration. Provided that, in cases where the stocks, etc. 
issued  by  the  corporation  that  has  filed  an  application  for  initial    listing  are  not 
registered electronically, it may be replaced first with the application documents for the 
registration or documents related to the issuance of the stocks, etc.; 

5.  The  written  confirmation  on  the  non-existence  of  parties  in  special  relationship, 

including the affiliates;   

6.  The opinion letter of main creditor bank;   

7.  The investment status confirmation of stakeholders; 

8.  The agreement for transfer agent services (referring to the agreement entered with the 
transfer agent for the provision of transfer agent services, etc.; the same hereinafter);   

9.  A copy of the appointment contract for the designated advisor; 

10. The KONEX Market listing agreement; 

11.   The  written  small  and  medium  enterprise  certificate  pursuant  to  Article  2  of  the 

Framework Act on Small and Medium Enterprises; 

12. In addition, other documents that are deemed necessary by the Exchange. 

(4) In addition to the documents in paragraph (3), a corporation that conducts a public offering 
6 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
or private placement after filing the application for initial listing shall submit the documents in 
the following subparagraphs by the day before the date of initial listing: (amended on April 17, 
2019) 

1.  Corporate  registration  (referring  the  those  that  reflects  the  results  of  the  issuance  of 

securities through public offering or private placement); 

2.  The  summary  table  of  shareholder  list  or  summary  table  of  subscription/assignment 

statement; 

3.  A    copy of the contact in relation with the issuance of securities including underwriting 
of securities, brokerage, arrangement, or proxy for public offering or private placement 
of securities, or acquisition of securities; 

4.  Documents verifying the payment of subscription money;   

5.  .In addition, other documents that the Exchange deems necessary. 

(5)  If  the  Exchange  deems  it  unavoidable,  the  submission  of  documents  under  each 
subparagraph of paragraph (3) may be deferred until the day before the date of initial listing. 
(Amended on April 17, 2019) 

(6) A corporation that intends to apply for initial listing on the KONEX Market before the end 
of the business year in which the date of merger, etc. falls pursuant to each subparagraph of 
Article 165-4 of the Act shall additionally submit financial statements for the latest fiscal year 
reflecting the effects of the merger, etc. and a review report by an external auditor [June 26, 
2014] 

§13. Par Value 

(1) “Amount stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in [§13(1)5] of the Regulation shall refer to 
any of following subparagraphs: 

1.  KRW 100, 200, 500, 1000 or 2,500; and 

2.  KRW 5,000. 

(2) Paragraph (1) shall apply mutatis mutandis to the case of stock split or reverse stock split 
among the reasons for listing changes pursuant to [§19]of the Regulations. 

§13-2. [Deleted on June 11, 2015] 

7 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
§13-3. Documents to Be Submitted by Technology Evaluation Corporation 

(1) “Application for KONEX Market initial listing examination stipulated in the Enforcement   
Rules (hereinafter referred to as “the application for initial listing examination”) in the main 
sentence of the part other than each subparagraph in [§13-2(2)] of the Regulation shall refer to 
[Listing Form No. 22] and “listing agreement by designated institutional investors (hereinafter 
referred  to  as  “the  listing  agreement”)”  shall  refer  to  [Listing  Form  No.  23].  (Amended  on 
December 29, 2016) 

(2) “Bonus issues stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in [§13-2(2)3] of the Regulation shall 

mean any of the following subparagraphs: 

1.  Capitalization of reserve pursuant to Article 46 of the Commercial Act; and 

2.  Transfer into capital pursuant to Article 30 of the Assets Revaluation Act. 

(3) “Documents stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in [§13-2(2)4] of the Regulation shall 
refer to  documents, issued by the Korea Securities Depository (KSD), which can prove the 
mandatory holding of stocks, etc. of designated institutional investors. Provided that, if stocks, 
etc. issued by the technology evaluation corporations is not registered electronically yet, they 
may  be  replaced  with  a  certificate  of  storage  of  the  stocks,  etc.  owned  by  the  designated 
institutional investors. [September 10, 2019] 

(4) “Documents specified in the Enforcement Rules” in [§13-2(2)5] of the Regulation shall 
refer to each of the following subparagraphs: (Amended on December 29, 2016; April 17, 2019) 

1.  Documents falling under [§12(3)] (excluding documents under subparagraphs 5 and 9); 

and 

2.  Documents falling under [§12(4) and (6)]. 

(5) If the Exchange deems it unavoidable, the submission of documents under paragraph (4)1 
may be deferred until the day before the date of initial listing. (Amended on September 10, 
2019) 

[June 30, 2015] 

§13-4.Advice from Expert Group, etc. 

(1)  In  examining  a  technology  evaluation  corporation  that  applied  for  initial  listing,  the 
Exchange  may  request  an  expert  group  to  provide  advice  on  the  professional  and  objective 
information on the technology of industry and the relevant field to which the corporation that 
applied for initial listing belongs. (Amended on December 29, 2016) 

(2) The Exchange may hold an expert meeting if it deems necessary to consult the expert 
group pursuant to paragraph (1). 

[June 30, 2015] 

8 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
§13-5.Calculation of Number of Investors Participating in Crowdfunding, etc. 

(1)“Requirements stipulated in  the  Enforcement  Rules” in  the proviso to  [§13-2(3)2] of the 
Regulation shall refer to the completion of a training course for listing support established by 
the Exchange. [June 19, 2017] 

(2)  Pursuant  to  the  latter  part  of  [§13-2(3)3]  of  the  Regulation,  the  number  of  investors 
participating in crowdfunding shall be calculated by subtracting the number of persons falling 
under each of the following subparagraphs from the number of investors who have invested in 
stocks through the online small investment brokerage (hereinafter referred to as  “the online 
small investment brokerage”) stated in [§2(18)] of the Regulation: (Amended on June 10, 2016) 

      1.An investor whose investment amount is less than KRW 500,000; 

      2.A person who falls under Article 11(1)2 of the Enforcement Decree of the Act; and 

      3.Other  persons  that  the  Exchange  deems  it  reasonable  not  to  include  in  the  number  of 

investors participating in crowdfunding. 

(3)The  number  of  investors  participating  in  crowdfunding  pursuant  to  paragraph  (2)  shall 
include at least two (2) persons who meet all the following subparagraphs: [June 10, 2020] 

      1. Must be a person who falls under any of the subparagraphs of Article 118-17(2) of the 

Enforcement Decree of the Act (including foreigners equivalent thereto); and 

      2.The investment amount must be at least KRW 10 million. 

[December 29, 2016] 

§13-6. Documents for Initial Listing of Crowdfunding Corporation 

(1)“Documents specified in the Enforcement Rules” in [§13-2(4)3] of the Regulation shall refer 
to each of the following documents: (Amended on June 19, 2017; April 17, 2019; June 10, 
2020) 

      1. Documents falling under [§12(3) (excluding documents under subparagraphs 5 and 9), 

(4), and (6)]; 

      2.In the  case of a corporation that issued securities through the online small  investment 
brokerage after applying for initial listing, documents falling under each of the following 
subparagraphs  related  to  the  issuance  of  the  securities  concerned.  In  such  case,  the 
documents concerned shall be submitted by the day before the date of initial listing: 

            a. Documents under [§12(4)1, 2, 4, and 5; and 

9 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
            b. A copy of the contract concluded in relation to the issuance of securities through the 

online small investment brokerage. 

      3.If  the  stocks  issued  by  the  online  small  investment  brokerage  fall  under  a  class  stock 
stated in the main sentence of [§13-2(3)2] of the Regulation, a document confirming that 
the conversion of the class stock into common stock has been completed prior to applying 
for initial listing; 

      4.In the case of a KSM-registered crowdfunding corporation stated in the proviso to [§13-
2(3)2] of the Regulations, documents falling under each of the following subparagraphs: 

            a. Documents confirming that 6 months have passed since registration with the KSM; 

            b. Documents proving that the corporation has completed the training course for listing 

support stated in [§13-5(1)]. 

      5.In the case of a corporation that has been recommended for listing on the KONEX market 
by a recommendation institution (hereinafter referred to as “recommendation institution”) 
pursuant  to  [§13-2(5)]  of the Regulation,  the KONEX Market  Listing  Recommendation 
Letter of [Listing Form No. 11-1]. 

(2)Notwithstanding paragraph (1), the submission of documents falling under paragraph (1)1, 
may  be  deferred  until  the  day  before  the  date  of  initial  listing  if  the  Exchange  deems 
unavoidable. 

[December 29, 2016] 

§13-7.Recommendation Institutions 

“Recommendation  institution  prescribed  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  [§13-2(5)]  of  the 
Regulation shall refer to an institution falling under any of the following subparagraphs: 

      1. The Korea Credit Guarantee Fund under the Credit Guarantee Fund Act; 

2. The Korea Technology Finance Corporation under the Technology Guarantee Fund Act; 

      3. Industrial Bank of Korea under the Industrial Bank of Korea Act; 

      4.Korea Growth Investment Management Co., Ltd. registered as a specialized private 

equity investment business pursuant to Article 249-3 of the Act; or 

      5.The Center for Creative Economy Innovation under Article 24-4(1) of the Enforcement 

Decree of the Framework Act on Science and Technology. 

[December 29, 2016] 

10 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
§14.Postponement of Notification of Results of Initial Listing Application, etc. 
(Amended on December 29, 2016) 

(1) “Documents prescribed in the Enforcement Rules” in the proviso to [§15(2)] of the 
Regulation shall refer to documents classified as follows:   

1.  In the case of a corporation that has applied for initial listing pursuant to [§12(1)] of 
the  Regulation:  Application  for  initial  listing,  a  listing  eligibility  report,  and  documents 
stated in each subparagraph of [§12(2)] of the Regulation; 

2.  In the case of a technology evaluation corporation that has applied for initial listing 
pursuant to [§13-2(1)] of the Regulation: Application for initial listing, a request for initial 
listing examination, a listing agreement and documents stated in each subparagraph of [§13-
2(2)] of the Regulation; and 

3.  In the case of a crowdfunding corporation that has applied for initial listing pursuant   
to [§13-2(3)] of the Regulation: Application for initial listing, a request for initial listing 
examination, and documents stated in each subparagraph of [§13-2(4)] of the Regulation. 

(2) “Other  reasons  prescribed  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  the  proviso  to  [§15(2)]  of  the 
Regulation shall refer to the reason in each of the following subparagraphs: (Amended on 
June 30, 2016; December 29, 2016) 

1.  In case where significant business matters such as suspension of business activities, 
occurrence of a disaster or change in assets equivalent to 10/100 or more of equity capital 
or other equivalent matters are discovered during the examination period and the Exchange 
deems that additional examination is necessary; 

      2.In case where the number of corporations applying for initial listing increases in a short 

period of time or it is necessary to finalize financial statements; 

      3.In case where the deliberation of the Committee is extended or there is an application for 
challenge against a Committee member (limited to technology evaluation corporations that 
have applied for initial listing pursuant to [§13-2(1)] of the Regulation). 

§15.Cancellation of Results of Initial Listing Examination 

“Other cases recognized by the Exchange as having a significant impact on the results of the 
initial listing examination” in [§16(1)4)] of the Regulation shall refer to each of the following 
subparagraphs: 

      1. In case where the appointment contract for the designated advisor is terminated; and 

      2. In other case where the Exchange deems it necessary for the public interest and investor 

protection. 

11 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
§16.Procedure for Appeal against Results of Listing Examination, etc. 

(1)In the case of an objection pursuant to [§17] of the Regulation, the interested party under 
any  of  the  following  subparagraphs  must  file  an  objection  within  30  days  from  the  date  of 
decision by the Exchange:(Amended on June 30, 2016; December 29, 2016) 

      1.Representative Director of the corporation; or 

      2. Designated advisor (excluding technology evaluation corporations that have applied for 
initial listing pursuant to [§13-2(1)] of the Regulation and crowdfunding corporations that 
have  applied  for  initial  listing  pursuant  to  paragraph  (3)  of  the  same  Article;  the  same 
hereinafter in paragraph (2)2. 

(2)Each  of  the  following  documents  shall  be  submitted  at  the  time  of  filing  the  objection 
pursuant to paragraph (1): 

      1.A statement of reasons for objecting to the decisions of the Exchange and documentation 

of evidence thereof; 

      2. The opinion letter of the designated advisor; and 

3. Other documents that the Exchange deems necessary in relation to the objection.   

(3)In  cases  where  an  official  objection  has  been  filed,  the  Exchange  shall  hold  a  hearing 
procedure within 30 days from the filing date concerned. In such case, the Exchange shall grant 
the  representative  of  the  corporation  that  filed  the  objection  an  opportunity  to  state  his/her 
opinion at least once. 

(4)The Exchange shall  make a decision on the  objection within 7 days  from  the end of the 
hearing procedure and, in such case, notify the interested parties of the result. 

(5)The interested parties shall not file another objection to the decision made in paragraph (4). 

(6)The hearing procedure under paragraph (3) shall be conducted by the following members: 

      1.Head of the KOSDAQ Market Division of the Exchange (hereinafter referred to as “the 

president"); 

      2.Two (2) Committee members determined by the president; and 

      3. No more than four (4) other persons deemed necessary by the Exchange. 

CHAPTER IV. ADMINISTRATION OF LISTED ISSUES 

12 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Section 1. Listing Change and Supplementary Listing 
[June 30, 2015] 

§17. Classification of Industry 

(1) The industry of a KONEX-listed corporation shall be classified into the division, sector and 
sub-sector  based  on  classification  and  codes  specified  in  [Annex  2]  based  on  the  Korean 
Standard  Industry  Classification  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  “the  Korean  Standard  Industrial 
Classification”) published by the Commissioner of the Statistics Korea in accordance with the 
Statistics Act. 

(2)If a KONEX-listed corporation is engaged in two (2) or more business or the type of 
business engaged in is not obvious, the following shall be applied: (Amended on March 20, 
2019) 

      1.In cases where a company is engaged in two (2) or more business, it shall be classified 
based on a business with a large portion of sales, but it may be classified based on a business 
yielding a large added value (amount) if deemed necessary; 

      2.In cases where it is difficult to apply the classification method stipulated in subparagraph 
1, the classification shall be made taking into account the number of employees or facilities, 
etc.; 

      3.In cases where it is difficult to classify an industry because the business details are unclear, 

it shall be classified under the other sector of similar industry division; 

      4.Notwithstanding paragraph (1), in the case of a holding company, if the sales of a specific 
industry  sector  are  fifty  (50)  percent  or  more  of  the  sales  in  the  consolidated  financial 
statements, it shall be classified based on the business of the industry concerned. However, 
a  holding  company  may  submit  documents  such  as  business  plan  in  relation  to  the 
classification of the industry, and the Exchange may classify the industry of the holding 
company  comprehensively  considering  the  realization  of  the  public  interest  and  the 
protection of investors. 

(3)The change of industry classification of a KONEX-listed corporation shall be made when 
the  corporation  falls  under  any  of  the  following  subparagraphs.  Provided  that  this  shall  not 
apply to cases where the Exchange deems that the industry reclassification is not necessary in 
consideration of the business history and future business prospects of the corporation, and the 
change of sub-sector within the same sector may not be made. 

      1.Case where it is necessary to change the industrial division subsequent to the revision of 

the Korean Standard Industrial Classification; 

      2.Case where the main business has been changed due to merger, spin-off, or transfer or 

takeover of business; 

      3.Case where there has been significant changes in the ranking of sales proportion of main 

13 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
products for the last two (2)fiscal years and the growth cannot be expected in the existing 
industry division, or when there is a significant change in the ranking of sales proportion 
of main products for the last fiscal year due to reorganization of business structure, change 
of  main  business,  etc.  and  the  Exchange  deems  the  reclassification  necessary  upon 
receiving the concerned listed corporation’s request for industry reclassification; 

      4.Case where the business is converted in accordance with the provisions of the Act; 

      5.In other cases where it is deemed necessary to change the business category. 

(4)The timing of reclassifying the industry sectors of KONEX-listed corporations shall be as 
follows: (Amended on June 19, 2019; March 20, 2019; March 11, 2020) 

      1.In the case of paragraph (3)1, 4, and 5, when the relevant fact is confirmed; 

      2.In the  case of paragraph (3)2, when  the document proving  that the  main business  has 
changed  due  to  the  relevant  merger,  spin-off,  or  transfer  or  takeover  of  business  was 
submitted; and 

      3.In the case of paragraph (3)3, the first trading day of the month in which five months are 
counted from the month following the month in which the account settlement date of the 
KONEX-listed  corporation  falls.  Provided  that,  if  a  KONEX-listed  corporation  fails  to 
submit a business report by the statutory submission deadline by falling under any of each 
subparagraph  of  [§24(4)],  the  Exchange  may  set  a  separate  time  for  the  industry 
reclassification for the corporation. 

(5)The Exchange may separately request materials needed for industry reclassification review 
from KONEX- listed corporations. 

(6)A  KONEX-listed  corporation  shall  submit  the  materials  required  for  the  industry 
reclassification review pursuant to paragraph (3)3 to the Exchange by the date of submission 
of the business report. Provided that, in cases where the time for changing the industry division 
is determined differently in accordance with the proviso to paragraph (4)3, the Exchange may 
set a separate submission date. (Amended on June 19, 2017) 

§18. Listing Change and Supplementary Listing 

(1) “Application for listing change/supplementary listing prescribed by the Enforcement 
Rules” [§19(1)] of the Regulation shall refer to [Listing Form No. 13] or [Listing Form No. 
13-1] and the attached documents shall refer to the following documents: (Amended on 
March 15, 2019; September 10, 2019; December 10, 2021) 

      1.Two (2) copies of the minutes of board meeting or general meetings of shareholders; 

      2.Two (2) certified copies of corporate register. Provided that, if the issuance of a 

certified copy of the corporate registration is not possible, the application documents for 
the issuance may be submitted first; 

14 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
      3.[Deleted on March 15, 2018] 

      4.Two (2) copies of certificate of issuance and registration; 

      5.In cases where new stocks are issued by way of the paid-in capital increase, etc., two (2) 

copies of documents verifying the payment of subscription money; 

            a. [Deleted on December 10, 2021] 
            b. [Deleted on December 10, 2021] 

      6.In the case of listing change or supplementary listing following the change of company 
name, stock split, and merger, etc., two (2) copies of documents verifying such fact; and 

      7.[Deleted on December 10, 2021] 

      8.Other documents that the Exchange deems necessary. 

(2) Applicants for listing change or supplementary listing shall submit the application for listing 
change or supplementary listing and attached documents to the Exchange by no later than five 
(5) business days prior to the scheduled date of listing change or supplementary listing. [March 
15, 2018] (Amended on September 10, 2019) 

(3) [Deleted on December 10, 2021] 

§19. Deferment of Listing Change and Supplementary Listing 

(1) “Cases stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in [§19(3)1] of the Regulation shall refer to 
any of the following cases: 

1. Case where a court decision or ruling on a lawsuit related to the validity of issuance of 
new stocks is being made, and the Exchange deems that there is little or no possibility of 
court refuting the validity of issuance of new stocks; and 

2. Case where the Exchange acknowledges that the trading safety would not be undermined 
by the listing change or supplementary listing in light of such factors as the reason for the 
lawsuit related to the validity of issuance of new stocks. 

(2)In the case of filing an official objection pursuant to [§19(4)] of the Regulation, the applicant 
for listing change or supplementary listing shall submit to the Exchange the notice of objection 
in  accordance  with  [Listing  Form  No.  14],  with  the  documents  in  each  of  the  following 
subparagraphs attached: 

      1.Documents related to the lawsuit on the validity of new stock issuance; 

      2.Opinion  letters  of  experts  in  the  concerned  fields,  such  as  the  lawyer,  certified  public 

account, and appraiser; and 

15 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
      3. Other documents related to the notice of objection, which the Exchange deems necessary. 

(3)Upon receiving an official objection stated in paragraph (2), provided that there is no special 
reason, the Exchange shall call a meeting of the Committee for the deliberation on whether to 
postpone the listing change or supplementary listing, within fifteen (15) days of receiving the 
objection. In such cases, the Exchange may give the representative of the applicant for listing 
change or supplementary listing an opportunity to present opinions. 

(4)The Exchange shall decide whether to postpone the listing change or supplementary listing 
within three (3) days from the date of deliberation of the Committee under paragraph (3). 

(5)The  provisions  of  [§27(8)  and  (9)]  shall  apply  mutatis  mutandis  to  the  case  of  official 
objection  against  the  postponement  of  listing  change  or  supplementary  listing  pursuant  to 
[§19(4)]. (Amended on June 26, 2014) 

§20. Shelf-listing 

(1) The application for shelf-listing pursuant to [§20(1)] of the Regulation shall refer to [Listing 
Form No. 15].   

(2) The written notice on issuance of new stocks pursuant to [§20 (2)] of the Regulation shall 
refer to [Listing Form 16] and the document to be attached shall be each of the followings: 
(Amended on September 10, 2019) 

1. Certificate of issuance and registration;   

2. A certified copy of corporate register. In this case, it can be submitted within 7 days after 
the registration of change; 

3. Written request to issue new stocks, a copy of conversion request or document proving 
exercise of stock options; and 

4. Other documents that the Exchange deems necessary. 

Section 2. Obligations of Listed Corporations, etc. 
[June 30, 2015] 

§21. Matters to Be Entered in Corporate Status Report, etc. 

(1) Designated advisors shall enter the following matters in the corporate status report under 
Article 25 (1) of the Regulations: 

      1. Overview of corporation; 

16 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
      2.Details  of  business  (including  matters  related  to  prediction  information  under  Article 

119(3) of the Act); 

      3. Financial matters: and 

      4.Other matters that the Exchange deems necessary for investor protection. 

(2) Designated advisors shall submit the corporate status report within forty-five (45) days after 
the  lapse  of  half-year  period  of  the  relevant  business  year  of  the  corporation  in  charge. 
(Amended on June 30, 2015p; April 17, 2019) 

(3) Notwithstanding paragraph (2), if the corporation in charge is a KONEX-listed corporation 
that  falls  under  any  of  the  following  items,  it  may  not  submit  a  corporate  status  report: 
(Amended on April 17, 2019) 

      1.In the case where the corporation is not listed on the KONEX market as of the end of the 

first half of the relevant business year; 

      2.In the case where the corporation falls under [§28(1) and (2)] of the Regulation; or 

      3.In the case where the corporation submits a semi-annual report. 

(4)Paragraphs (1) through (3) shall apply mutatis mutandis to the corporate status report of the 
relevant corporation pursuant to [§25(4)] of the Regulation. [June 30, 2015] 

§22. [Deleted on July 11, 2014] 

Section 3. Assignment and Change of Corporation Division 
[June 30, 2015] 

§22-2. Change of Corporation Division 

(1) The change of corporation division pursuant to [§26(3)] of the Regulations shall be put 
into effect on the day after the date of conclusion of the appointment contract for the 
designated advisor (in the case of the appointment contract becoming effective after the date 
of conclusion of the appointment contract for the designated advisor, on the day of the 
effective date). 

(2)The change of corporation division pursuant to [§26(3)] of the Regulation is limited to the 
change from the Startups Division or the Crowdfunding Corporation Division to the Ordinary 
Corporation Division. (Amended on December 29, 2016)

[June 30, 2015] 

Section 4. Designated Institutional Investor 
[June 30, 2015] 

§22-3. Application for Designation of Designated Institutional Investor 

“Application  for  designation  of  a  designated  institutional  investor”  in  [§26-4(2)]  of  the 
Regulation shall refer to [Listing Form No. 24] 

[June 30, 2015] 

§22-4. Qualifications of Designated Institutional Investor 

(1)  “Period  specified  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  the  proviso  in  the  part  other  than  each 
subparagraph in [§26-5] of the Regulation shall be as follow: (Amended on June 19, 2017) 

1.Revocation of the qualification of designated institutional investor pursuant to [§26-7(2)] 
of the Regulation: one (1) year. 

      2.Revocation  of  designated  institutional  investor  qualifications  under  [§26-7(3)]  of  the 

Regulation: three (3) years. 

(2)“Professional manpower prescribed in the Enforcement Rules” prescribed in [§26-5(2)] of 
the  Regulation  shall  mean  a  person  who  falls  under  any  of  the  following  subparagraphs: 
(Amended on March 8, 2021) 

      1.A person who has at least 3 years of experience in corporate financing pursuant to Article 

68(2) of the Enforcement Decree of the Act; or 

      2.A person who falls under each subparagraph of Article 23(7)1 of the Enforcement Decree 

of the Venture Investment Promotion Act. 

[June 30, 2015] 

§22-5. Appeal against Result of Designation of Designated Institutional Investor 

(1)In case of an objection pursuant to [§26-6(2)] of the Regulation, the applicant for designation 
of  designated  institutional  investor  shall  file  an  objection  within  30  days  from  the  date  of 
decision of the Exchange. 

(2)An applicant for designation of a designated institutional investor shall submit the following 
18 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
documents when filing an objection under paragraph (1): 

      1.A statement of reasons for objecting to the decisions of the Exchange and documentation 

of evidence thereof; and 

      2. Other documents that the Exchange deems necessary in relation to the objection.   

(3)In cases where an official objection has been filed, the Exchange shall hold a Committee 
meeting within 30 days from the filing date concerned. In such case, the Exchange shall grant 
the representative of the applicant for designation of designated institutional investor that filed 
the objection an opportunity to state opinion at least once. 

(4)The  Exchange  shall  make  a  decision  on  the  objection  within  7  days  from  the  date  of 
deliberation of the Committee and, in such case, notify the interested parties of the result. 

(5)The  applicant  for  designation  of  designated  institutional  investor  shall  not  file  another 
objection to the decision made in paragraph(4). 

[June 30, 2015] 

§22-6. Procedure for Appeal against Measures to Designated Institutional Investors 

(1)In the case of an objection against measures taken by the Exchange pursuant to [§26-7(2) 
and (3)]] of the Regulation, the designated institutional investor shall file an objection within 
seven (7) days from the date of receipt of the notice.(Amended on June 19, 2017) 

(2)Each  of  the  following  documents  shall  be  submitted  at  the  time  of  filing  the  objection 
pursuant to paragraph (1): 

      1.A statement of reasons for objecting to the decisions of the Exchange and documentation 

of evidence thereof; 

      2. Other documents that the Exchange deems necessary in relation to the objection.   

(3)In cases where an official objection has been filed, the Exchange shall hold a Committee 
meeting within fifteen (15) days from the filing date concerned. In such case, the Exchange 
shall grant the representative of the designated institutional investor that filed the objection an 
opportunity to state opinion at least once. 

(4)The Exchange shall decide whether to take action against designated institutional investors 
within 3 days from the date of deliberation by the Committee. 

[June 30, 2015] 

19 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Section 5. Suspension and Resumption of Trading 
(Amended on April 28, 2022) 

§22-7. [Deleted on April 28, 2022] 

§23. Suspension and Resumption of Trading 

(1)  The  period  of  trading  suspension  of  stocks  suspended  in  trading  pursuant  to 
[§27(1)1(excluding cases of listing on the KOSPI or KOSDAQ market and  being acquired) 
and  2]  of  the  Regulations  shall  be  from  the  date  on  which  the  fact  falling  under  any  of 
subparagraphs of [§28(1) and (2)] of the Regulation is confirmed to the date of resolving the 
reasons for delisting in accordance with [§29(4)] of the Regulation or [§30(3) through (5)] of 
the Regulation. Provided that, if an improvement period is granted pursuant to [§27(4)], the 
Exchange  may  cancel  the  suspension  of  trading  during  the  improvement  period  after 
deliberation by the Committee. <Amended on June 30, 2015; April 17, 2019; April 28, 2022) 

(2) Notwithstanding the main sentence of paragraph (1), the period of trading suspension shall 
be  the  period  specified  in  each  subparagraph.  in  cases  falling  under  any  of  the  following 
subparagraphs,  Provided  that,  if  the  Exchange  deems  necessary  for  the  public  interest  and 
investor protection, the suspension may not be lifted: (Amended on July 11, 2014; June 30, 
2015; December 29, 2016; April 17, 2019; April 28, 2022) 

1.  Where  the  annual  report  under  [§27(1)1]  of  the  Regulation  is  not  submitted  by  the 
statutory submission deadline: The period from the day after the statutory submission 
deadline to the date of submitting the annual report; 

2.  Where  the  appointment  contract  for  a  designated  advisor  under  [§27(1)1]  of  the 
Regulation is cancelled: The period from the date of confirming the cancellation of the 
appointment contract for the designated advisor to the date of confirming a conclusion 
of an appointment contract for a designated advisor; 

3.  Cases falling under [§28(1)12 or 13] of the Regulation: The period from the date on 
which one (1) year has elapsed from the date of listing to the date of confirming the 
conclusion of the appointment contract for the designated advisor; and 

4.  Cases falling under [§28(2)2] of the Regulation: The period from the date of confirming 
the  relevant  cause  to  the  date  when  the  court  decides  to  commence  rehabilitation 
procedures. 

(3)The period of trading suspension of stocks suspended in trading pursuant to [§27(1)3] of the 
Regulation shall be as follows. (Amended on July 26, 2014; June 30, 2015; April 17, 2019; 
April 28, 2022) 

      1. In cases falling under the proviso to  [§28(1)7] of the Regulation, the period from the 
confirmation of the audit opinion on the financial statements of the latest business year until 

20 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
the decision on whether to delist or not; 

      1-2. In cases falling under [§24-2(1)1], the period from the date on which the relevant fact 
is  confirmed  through  disclosure,  etc.  pursuant  to  the  KONEX  Market  Disclosure 
Regulation until the date on which it is confirmed whether the relevant fact falls under the 
cause for delisting pursuant [§24-2(1)]; 

1-3.  In  cases  of  the  report  pursuant  to  [§6(5)(f)]  of  the  KONEX  Market  Disclosure 
Regulation, the period from the date of report to the date on which it is confirmed whether 
the corporation falls under the cause for delisting pursuant to [§28(1)14] of the Regulation; 

      2. In cases of the determination on whether or not a corporation is subject to deliberation 
by the Committee pursuant to [§29(1)] of the Regulation (excluding the case in [§28(2)2] 
of the Regulation;  the same  hereinafter in  subparagraph 3), the period from  the date on 
which the fact is confirmed pursuant to the same subparagraph of the same Article until the 
date on which it is decided whether or not the corporation is subject to deliberation by the 
Committee; 

      3. In cases of determining a corporation as being subject to deliberation by the Committee 
pursuant  to  [§29(1)]  of  the  Regulation,  the  period  from  the  date  of  determining  the 
corporation  as  being  subject  to  deliberation  by  the  Committee  pursuant  to  the  same 
paragraph of the same Article to the date of determining whether the corporation falls under 
a cause for delisting pursuant to paragraph (4) of the same Article; 

      4.  In  cases  where  the  Exchange  deems  necessary  for  investor  protection  and  market 
management after the court's decision to commence rehabilitation procedures, the period 
from the date of the decision concerned to suspend trading (including the suspension of 
trading under the proviso to  paragraph (2))until  the date of confirmation if the cause of 
delisting of the corporation concerned is recognized as resolved; 

      5.  In  cases  where  a  cause  for  trading  suspension  is  recognized  as  resolved  pursuant  to 
[§30(4) or (5)] of the Regulations after the termination of the period of cancellation of the 
suspension of trading, until the date of confirmation; 

      6.In  cases  where  a  corporation  files  bankruptcy  pursuant  to  Article  294  of  the  Debtor 
Rehabilitation and Bankruptcy Act, the period from the date on which the fact concerned 
is  confirmed  to  the  date  on  which  the  dissolution  of  the  relevant  cause  is  confirmed. 
Provided that, if the Exchange deems necessary, the suspension may be lifted 

      7. [Deleted on April 28, 2022] 

      8. In other cases that are deemed necessary for investor protection, one (1) day. Provided 

that if the Exchange deems necessary, the period may be extended. 

(4) The calculation of the period from paragraphs (1) through (3) shall be based on the trading 
day  (including  the  trading  suspension  date)  in  the  regular  market  stated  in[§4(2)1]  of  the 
KONEX Market Business Regulation. (Amended on April 17, 2019) 

(5) Paragraphs (1) and (2) shall not apply during the trading period pursuant to [§33] of the 
21 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Regulation. 

CHAPTER V. DELISTING 

§24. Application of Delisting Criteria 

(1)The Exchange shall disclose the detailed procedures  related to  the delisting of KONEX-
listed corporations as market guidance. 

(2)The auditor's confirmation document submitted in accordance with the proviso to [§28(1)7] 
of the Regulation shall be in accordance with [Listing Form No. 17]. 

(3)“Detailed  standards”  in  [§28(3)]  of  the  Regulation  shall  be  any  of  the  following 
subparagraphs. (Amended on April 17, 2019; October 14, 2019; December 10, 2021) 

      1.“Amount  specified  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  [§28(2)4(a)]  of  the  Regulation  shall 
refer to an amount corresponding to [§6/4c (in the case of officers, 3/100 or more of equity 
capital or KRW 10 billion or more of embezzlement and breach of trust] of the KONEX 
Market Disclosure Regulation; 

      2.Case  of  falling  under  the  criteria  for  delisting  when  taking  into  account  the  details  of 
matters breaching the accounting standards that have been confirmed through the annual 
report,  correction  of  annual  report,  details  of  accusation  by  the  prosecutor  and  result  of 
investigation by the Securities and  Futures Commission, or case where the fact  that the 
Financial Services Commission (FSC) or the Securities and Futures Commission has made 
a resolution to take measures of filing an accusation or informing to the prosecutor’s office 
of the KONEX-listed corporation for its violation of accounting standards is confirmed; 

      3.“Suspension of main business” shall refer to the cases falling under any of the following 
subparagraphs in which it is difficult to carry out a viable operation with the remaining part 
of business. In such case, the judgment on the main business shall be made based on the 
sales amount. Provided that, if it is deemed necessary, the added value (amount) may be 
used as the basis for such judgment: 

(a)      Discontinuation of the production and sales of main business.  In the case of a 
suspension due to labor disputes or natural disasters, it shall be limited to cases where 
the production and sales are discontinued for six (6) months or more; 

(b) Cancellation or return of the permit or license related to main business; 

(c) Where the main business has been taken over or has been transferred to the company 
established through spin-off or merger after spin-off (including the physical spin-off or 
merger after physical spin-off; the same hereinafter in this subparagraph); or 

22 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(d)  Other  cases  where  the  Exchange  recognizes  that  the  main  business  has  been 
effectively discontinued. 

(4) If a KONEX-listed corporation is not  able to submit its business report by the statutory 
submission deadline since it falls under any of the following subparagraphs within three (3) 
months  before  the  statutory  submission  deadline  of  the  business  report,  the  corporation 
concerned shall apply for an extension of the submission deadline, and the Exchange may apply 
the statutory submission deadline under [§28(1)1 and 7] of the Regulation by adding the period 
specified in each of the following subparagraphs:(Amended on March 11, 2020) 

1. In case where it is impossible for an auditor of a KONEX-listed corporation (including 
a  subsidiary  of  the  corporation)  to  conduct  an  audit  because  it  falls  under  any  of  the 
subparagraphs  of  [§13(2)]  of  the  Enforcement  Decree  of  the  External  Audit  of  Stock 
Companies, etc.: Within 3 months from the legal submission deadline for business reports; 
or 

      2.  In  other  cases  where  it  is  unavoidable  that  the  submission  of  a  business  report  of  a 
KONEX-listed  corporation  cannot  normally  be  made  within  the  statutory  submission 
deadline and the situation is recognized through approval by the FSC or the Securities and 
Futures Commission: Period until the date determined through approval, etc. by the FSC 
or the Securities and Futures Commission 

(5)  Notwithstanding  paragraph  (4),  a  KONEX-listed  corporation  falls  under  any  of  the 
subparagraphs of paragraph (4) within three months before the statutory submission deadline 
of the business report, and the Exchange recognizes that this situation is the main reason for 
not submitting the business report by the statutory submission deadline through the explanation 
of the corporation, the Exchange may apply the statutory submission deadline under [§28(1)1 
and 7] of the Regulation by adding the period specified in each of the subparagraphs concerned. 
[June 19, 2017] (Amended on March 11, 2020) 

(6) [Deleted on January 31, 2018] 

(7) [Deleted on January 31, 2018] 

(8) If, as a case where a KONEX-listed corporation files an objection to delisting pursuant to 
[§30] of the Regulation since it falls under the cause in the main sentence of [§28(1)7] of the 
Regulation  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  “the  audit  opinion-related  delisting  causes”),  an  audit 
opinion  on  the  audit  report  for  the  next  fiscal  year  of  the  corporation  that  submitted  the 
improvement plan to obtain the audit opinion of “unqualified” on the audit report of the next 
fiscal year does not fall under the audit opinion-related delisting causes, the cause for delisting 
concerned may be recognized as resolved. [March 20, 2019] (Amended on March 8, 2021) 

(9) In cases where the cause of each subparagraph of [§28(1)] (excluding subparagraph 10) or 
each subparagraph of [§28(2)] is resolved after the proviso to [§28(1)10] of the Regulation is 
applied, the cause in the main sentence of [§28(1)10] of the Regulation shall apply from the 
half year that comes after the date on which the cause is resolved. [April 28, 2022] 

23 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
§24-2. Methods of Applying Causes for Stock Distribution not Meeting Criteria 

(1)  Causes  for  not  meeting  the  stock  distribution  criteria  pursuant  to  [§28(1)7-2]  of  the 
Regulation  shall  be  applied  if  a  KONEX-listed  corporation  falls  under  all  the  following 
subparagraphs: (Amended on April 28, 2022) 

      1.In cases where the corporation falls under the causes for stock distribution not meeting 
criteria based on the register of shareholders, etc. as of the end of the latest fiscal year (if 
the register of shareholders is closed after the end of the latest fiscal year, it shall be as of 
the time of closure); and 

      2. In cases where the corporation has not proven that the causes for stock distribution not 
meeting criteria stated in subparagraph 1 have resolved within ten (10) days from the day 
after the statutory submission deadline for the business report for the latest fiscal year.   

(2)In relation to paragraph (1), a KONEX-listed corporation shall submit the summary of the 
register of shareholders in the [Listing Form No. 10] to the Exchange two (2) weeks before the 
statutory submission deadline for the business report (It can be submitted through the electronic 
disclosure system in accordance with [§29(1)] of the KONEX Market Disclosure Regulation). 

(3)“Those  that  are  difficult  to  be  considered  dispersed”  in  [§28(1)7-2(b)]  of  the  Regulation 
shall refer to common stocks in each of the following subparagraphs: (Amended on March 11, 
2020) 

      1. Treasury stocks; 

      2. Stocks held by major shareholders pursuant to Article 2/6(b) of the Act on Corporate 
Governance  of  Financial  Companies.  Provided  that,  common  stocks  held  by  a  person 
falling under any of the following subparagraphs are excluded: 

            (a)Venture capital stated in [§2(5)] of the Regulation; 

            (b) Professional investors stated in [§2(6)] of the Regulation; and 

(c) Employee stock ownership association pursuant to Article 2(4) of the Framework Act on 

Labor Welfare. 

[April 17, 2019] 

§24-3. Methods of Applying Causes for Delisting Due to Capital Impairment 

(1)  The  cause  under  [§28(1)14]  of  the  Regulation  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  the  “cause  for 
delisting due to capital impairment”) shall apply based on the audit report reported pursuant to 
[§6(5)(a)] of the KONEX Market Disclosure Regulation. In such cases, if there is a correction 
to the report, the cause shall apply based on the corrected details. 

(2)  The  cause  for  delisting  due  to  capital  impairment  shall  apply  based  on  the  financial 

24 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
statements pursuant to [§3(2)] of the Regulation and the fiscal year of the concerned financial 
statements. 

(3)  In cases  where a KONEX-listed corporation falling under the cause for delisting due to 
capital impairment has filed an objection against delisting pursuant to [§30] of the Regulation 
and submitted financial statements (based on consolidated financial statements for corporations 
subject to the preparation of consolidated financial statements) and an auditor’s report on these 
financial statements (limited to cases where the auditor’s opinion is unqualified), which prove 
that the relevant cause has been resolved, it may be deemed that the relevant cause has been 
resolved. 

(4) In cases where a KONEX-listed corporation has split off to convert into a holding company 
but the conversion has not been completed, the cause for delisting due to capital impairment 
shall not apply during the fiscal year in which the split-off has taken place and the following 
fiscal year. 

[April 28, 2022] 

§25. Listing Maintenance Review 

(1) The Exchange shall call a meeting of the Committee within twenty (20) days [when the 
concerned corporation falls under [§28(2)2] of the Regulation, within thirty (30) days]from the 
date of making a notification pursuant to [§29(2)] of the Regulation, (Amended on March 8, 
2021) 

(2)The Committee shall deliberate on whether the delisting criteria apply or not according to 
the following review criteria: (Amended on April 17, 2019) 

      1.Unfaithful disclosure 

(a) In view of the worsening investor confidence caused by the concerned unfaithful 
disclosure,  whether  it,  as  a  listed  corporation,  would  be  regarded  as  an  appropriate 
investment choice; 

      (b) The impact that the concerned unfaithful disclosure has on the business operation of the 

corporation; and 

      (c)Additionally, in relation to the concerned unfaithful disclosure, whether the delisting is 

necessary for the protection of the KONEX Market and investors. 

      2.  Reasons  for  the  application  for  commencement  of  rehabilitation  procedure  by  a 
corporation,  rejection  of  the  application  for  commencement  of  rehabilitation  procedure, 
cancellation of the decision for commencement of rehabilitation procedure, disapproval of 
rehabilitation plan, decision for cancellation of rehabilitation procedure, etc. by the court.   

      3. Falsification of documents relating to listing 

            (a) The significance on the listing examination and the effect on the investors that the 

25 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
falsified statement, etc. may have; and 

            (b)  Whether  or  not  a  KONEX-listed  corporation  made  the  false  statement,  etc. 

intentionally or by gross mistake. 

      4. Overall assessment pursuant to [§28(2)4] of the Regulation 

            (a) Whether or not the financial position would deteriorate due to the embezzlement or 

the breach of trust, etc.; 

            (b)Whether  or  not  the  operational  transparency  has  been  damaged  due  to  the 

embezzlement or the breach of trust, etc.; 

            (c)Whether or not the details of matters violating the disclosure obligation, including 
the violation of accounting standards and unfaithful disclosure, are of the significant 
nature; and 

            (d) In addition to subparagraphs 4(a) through 4(c), whether the delisting is necessary 

for the KONEX Market and investor protection. 

§26. [Deleted on July 11, 2014] 

§27. Appeal against Delisting and Deliberation thereof 

(1)“Cases stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in [§30(1)] of the Regulation shall refer to the 
cases falling under [§28(1)1, 5, 6, 9 and 11] of the Regulation. (Amended on January 31, 2018; 
March 11, 2020) 

(2)When a KONEX-listed corporation files  an official objection pursuant to [§30(2)] of the 
Regulation,  it shall submit  the following documents attached to  the official  objection under 
[Listing Form No.  18]:  (Amended on June 30, 2015; December 29, 2016;  March 20, 2019; 
December 10, 2021) 

      1. An improvement plan that includes plan to resolve the cause for delisting (in case of 
falling  under  audit  opinion-related  delisting  causes,  the  improvement  plan  to  resolve 
delisting cause by revising the audit opinion on the audit report of the relevant fiscal year 
or to receive an ‘unqualified’ audit opinion on the audit report of the following fiscal year); 

      2. Opinion statements issued by experts in the relevant fields, including lawyers, certified 
public  accountants,  and  appraisers,  etc.  (excluding  KONEX-listed  corporations  falling 
under the causes in [§28(1)7-2, 10, 12 and 13] of the Regulation); and 

      3. Other documents that the Exchange deems necessary in relation to the official objection. 

(3)When an official objection under paragraph (2) has been filed, unless there is any special 

26 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
reason,  the  Exchange  shall  call  a  meeting  of  the  Committee  within  twenty  (20)  days  of 
receiving  the  concerned  objection  and  make  a  deliberation  on  the  matters  in  each  of  the 
following  subparagraphs.  In  such  cases,  the  Exchange  shall  grant  the  representative  of  the 
concerned  KONEX-listed  corporation  an  opportunity  to  present  the  opinion:  (Amended  on 
March 20, 2019; June 10, 2020; March 8, 2021) 

      1.Whether to delist the concerned stock; 

      2.Feasibility  of  the  improvement  plan(in  case  of  falling  under  audit  opinion-related 
delisting  causes,  the  improvement  plan  shall  indicate  the  possibility  to  resolve  delisting 
cause  by  revising  the  audit  opinion  on  the  audit  report  of  the  relevant  fiscal  year  or  to 
receive  an  ‘unqualified’  audit  opinion  on  the  audit  report  of  the  following  fiscal  year), 
whether or not to grant the improvement period, and if granted, the length of improvement 
period; and 

      3.Whether to suspend the trading of concerned stock and if suspended, the period of trade 

suspension. 

(4) The Exchange shall decide whether the relevant stock will be delisted or not or whether an 
improvement  period  will  be  granted  or  not,  etc.,  within  three  (3)  days  from  the  date  of 
deliberation of the Committee, and if an improvement period is granted, unless there is any 
special reason, the length of such period shall not exceed the period in each of the following 
subparagraphs: (Amended on November 13, 2013; June 30, 2015; December 29, 2016; March 
20, 2019; April 17, 2019; April 28, 2022) 

      1. In the case of falling [§28(1)7, 7-2, 12, 13, 14, and (2)2] of the Regulation: Within one 

(1) year; and 

      2.Causes for delisting other than subparagraph 1: Within six (6) months 

(5) During the improvement period, the Exchange may check the progress in implementing the 
improvement plan through such means as annual reports and quarterly reports, etc. (Amended 
on November 13, 3013; June 10, 2020) 

(6)  A  KONEX-listed  corporation  that  has  been  granted  an  improvement  period  pursuant  to 
paragraph (4) shall submit the documents in each of the following subparagraphs within fifteen 
(15) days after the end of the improvement period (in the case of filing an application pursuant 
to [§30(5)3] of the Regulation before the expiration of the improvement period, the date of 
such application). Provided that this shall not be the case for a KONEX-listed corporation that 
falls under causes stated in [§28(1)12 and 13] of the Regulation: (Amended on June 30, 2015; 
December 29, 2016; March 20, 2019; April 17, 2019; June 10, 2020; March 8, 2021; December 
10, 2021; April 28, 2022) 

      1.An implementation statement of the improvement plan; 

      2.A written confirmation on the outcome of implementation of the improvement plan issued 
by experts in the relevant fields such as lawyers, certified public accountants, or appraisers 
(excluding  the  KONEX-listed  corporations  falling  under  [§28(1)7-2  and  10]  of  the 
Regulation). In such cases, in the case of submitting the improvement plan to receive an 
27 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
“unqualified”  audit  opinion  on  the  audit  report  of  the  following  fiscal  year  pursuant  to 
paragraph (2)1 due to falling under audit opinion-related delisting causes, it shall be the 
audit  report  of  the  relevant  fiscal  year,,  and  in  the  case  of  falling  under  the  cause  for 
delisting due to capital impairment, it shall be the financial statements under [§24-3(3)] and 
the auditor’s report on these financial statements; and 

      3.  Other  documents  that  the  Exchange  deems  necessary  for  the  deliberation  on  the 

implementation of the improvement plan. 

(7) Unless there is  any special reason, the Exchange shall  call a meeting  of the Committee 
within twenty (20) days from the submission date of documents under paragraph (6) to make 
a deliberation on whether the improvement plan was implemented and whether or not to delist 
the stocks and decide whether the concerned stock will be delisted or not within three (3) days 
from the date of the deliberation. (Amended on June 30, 2015; December 29, 2016; June 10, 
2020; March 8, 2021) 

(8) When the Exchange makes a decision pursuant to paragraphs (4) or (7), it shall notify the 
KONEX-listed  corporation  concerned  and  the  designated  advisor  in  charge  (excluding 
corporations  in  Startups  Division  and  Crowdfunding  Corporation  Division:  the  same 
hereinafter  in  [§28(1)2  and  (2)2])of  the  details  of  the  decision  in  writing  without  delay. 
(Amended on June 30, 2015; December 29, 2016) 

(9)  KONEX-listed  corporations  cannot  file  another  official  objection  to  the  decision  on 
delisting under paragraph (4) or (7).   

(10) ”Case stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in [§30(6)] of the Regulation shall refer to the 
case  falling  under  any  of  the  following  subparagraphs:  [March  8,  2021]  (Amended  on 
December 10, 2021; April 28, 2022) 

      1. Cases where an official objection is filed with the documents in each subparagraph of 
paragraph  (2)  by  falling  under  the  audit  opinion-related  delisting  causes  and  then  the 
Exchange  grants  an  improvement  period.  In  such  cases,  the  Exchange  shall  grant  an 
improvement period from the day after the statutory submission deadline to the 10th day for 
the business report for the fiscal year following the fiscal year corresponding to the audit 
opinion-related delisting causes;   

2. Cases where, once after an audit opinion subject to delisting was issued, the Exchange 
decides to maintain the listing because the revised audit opinion on the audit report of the 
relevant fiscal year or the audit opinion on the audit report of the fiscal year following the 
relevant fiscal year does not correspond to the audit opinion-related delisting causes; 

3.  Cases  where  an  official  objection  is  filed  with  the  documents  specified  in  each 
subparagraph  of  paragraph  (2)  for  not  satisfying  the  distribution  requirement  and  the 
Exchange decides to grant an improvement period. In such cases, the Exchange shall grant 
the improvement period from the day after the statutory submission deadline to the 10th day 
for the business report for the fiscal year following the fiscal year in which the cause for 
not satisfying the distribution requirement occurred;   

4.  Cases  where  the  Exchange  decides  to  maintain  the  listing  since  it  confirmed  that  a 
28 

 
   
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
cause for not satisfying the distribution requirement had been removed; 

5. Cases where an official objection is filed with the documents in each subparagraph of 
paragraph  (2)  by  falling  under  the  cause  for  delisting  due  to  capital  impairment  and  the 
Exchange decides to grant an improvement period. In such cases, the Exchange shall grant 
an improvement period from the day after the statutory submission deadline of the business 
report for the fiscal year following the fiscal year in which the relevant cause occurred to 
the 10th day; or 

6. Cases where, after the cause for delisting due to capital impairment occurred, financial 
statements  (based  on  consolidated  financial  statements  for  corporations  subject  to  the 
preparation of consolidated financial statements) and an auditor’s report on these financial 
statements (limited to cases where the auditor’s opinion is unqualified), which prove that 
the relevant cause has been resolved, are submitted and the Exchange decides to maintain 
the listing. 

§28. Documents to be Filed with Application for Delisting, etc. 

(1)  “Application  for  delisting  stipulated  in  the  Enforcement  Rules.”  in  [§31(1)]  of  the 
Regulation shall refer to the [Listing Form No. 19], and supplementary document shall refer to 
those stated in each of the following subparagraphs: (Amended on February 3, 2014; June 30, 
2015; December 29, 2019) 

      1.Two (2) copies of the minutes on special resolution of general meeting of shareholders 
concerned with the delisting (in the case of application for delisting pursuant to [§28(1)11] 
of the Regulation, the minutes of meeting of the Board of Directors: the same hereinafter 
in paragraph (2)1); and 

      2.Two (2) copies of the consent on delisting of the designated advisor in charge. 

(2)“Application  for  delisting  stipulated  in  the  Enforcement  Rules.”  in  [§31(2)]  of  the 
Regulation shall refer to the [Listing Form No. 20], and supplementary document shall refer to 
those stated in each of the following subparagraphs: 

      1.Two (2) copies of the minutes on special resolution of general meeting of shareholders 
of different classes of stocks concerned with the delisting; and 

      2.Two (2) copies of the consent on delisting of the designated advisor in charge. 

(3)When an application for delisting noted in [§31(1) & (2)] of the Regulation has been filed, 
unless there is  any  special  reason, the Exchange  shall call a meeting of the Committee and 
make a deliberation on the matters noted in each of the following subparagraphs within fifteen 
(15) days of receiving the concerned application. Provided that, this provision shall not apply 
to the case under [§28(1)11] of the Regulation: (Amended on February 3, 2014; April 15, 2019; 
June 10, 2020) 

      1.Whether to delist the concerned stock; 

29 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
      2.Whether  or  not  the  largest  shareholder,  etc.  (including  the  joint  holders  under  Article 
141(1) of the Enforcement Decree of the Act, while excluding the relevant KOSDAQ-listed 
corporation;  hereinafter  referred  to  as  “the  largest  shareholder”  in  this  Article)  have 
faithfully observed the procedures for shareholder protection by such means of acquiring 
stocks  from  the  shareholders  who  held  the  concerned  stocks  before  the  application  for 
delisting (including tender offers and other means equivalent thereto), or guaranteeing the 
acquisition of the concerned stocks fora specified period after the delisting; and 

      3.In addition, whether matters necessary for the public interest and the investor protection, 
such as the share ownership ratio of the largest shareholder (referring to the ratio calculated 
based on the number of shares produced by subtracting the number of treasury shares from 
the total number of issued shares) and tender offer conditions, are fulfilled. 

(4)Exchange shall decide whether to delist within three (3) days from the date of deliberation 
of the Committee pursuant to paragraph (3). 

CHAPTER VI. SUPPLEMENTARY PROVISIONS 

§29. Calculation of Period 

(1) The period shall be calculated in accordance with any of the following methods, except as 
otherwise provided in these Enforcement Rules: (Amended on April 28, 2022) 

      1.The first day of the period shall not be included in the computation; 

      2.If a period is calculated by the day, the computation shall be made based on the business 
day (referring to days excluding Saturdays, public holidays under the Regulations on Public 
Holidays of Government Offices and Labor Day under Act on Establishment of Labor Day); 
or 

      3.When a period is calculated by the week, month or year, it shall be computed according 

to the calendar. 

(2)  Notwithstanding  to  paragraph  (1)2,  [§20(2)2],  [§21(2)],  [§24-2(1)2],  [§27(10)]  and 
[§28(1)2 and 7] of the Regulation shall be computed according to the calendar. (Amended on 
April 17, 2019; April 28, 2022) 

§30. Listing Fees and Annual Dues 

The exemption criteria for listing fees and annual dues under the proviso to [§37(1)] of the 
Regulation and the imposition criteria and the payment timing of listing fees and annual dues 

30 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
under  [§37(2)]  of  the  Regulation  and  other  necessary  matters  shall  apply  as  stipulated  in 
[Annex 3]. 

§31. Public Opinion Gathering 

Public  opinion  gathering  pursuant  to  [§37-2]  of  the  Regulation  shall  be  governed  by  the 
provisions  of  [§5]  of  the  Internal  Regulations  Management  Regulation  and  [§6]  of  the 
Regulations Management Regulation 

[May 6, 2020] 

31 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
ADDENDA 
(September 13, 2013)   

§1. Effective Date   

These Enforcement Rules shall become effective on September 17, 2013. 

§2. Applicable Case Concerning the Corporate Status Report   

In  the  case  of  submitting  the  semi-annual  report  or  the  quarterly  report  pursuant  to  Article 
160of the Act, it shall be deemed that the corporate status report pursuant to [§21] has been 
submitted.   

§3. Interim Measures on the KONEX Market Listing and Disclosure Committee   

A  committee  for  electing  the  designated  advisor  pursuant  to  the  former  KOSDAQ  Market 
Listing Regulation as of the effective date of these Enforcement Rules shall be construed as 
the KONEX Market Listing and Disclosure Committee pursuant to these Enforcement Rules 
until the KONEX Market Listing and Disclosure Committee are composed.   

§4. Applicable Case Concerning the Listing Fees and Annual Dues     

The listing fees pursuant to Annex 3 shall apply starting with the company that submits the 
application for initial listing and listing change (supplementary listing) after the date separately 
determined by the Exchange, and the annual dues shall be calculated and apply from the date 
separately determined by the Exchange. (Amended on June 11, 2015; June 27, 2016; June 19, 
2017; June 26, 2018; June 10, 2020; April 28, 2022) 

§5. Amendment of Other Regulations   

A part of the Enforcement Rules of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation shall be amended 
as in the followings:     

- Chapter V-II ([§36-2 through §36-37]) shall be deleted;   
- Listing Fees and Annual Dues stipulated in subparagraph 4(h) of Annex 4 shall be deleted; 
and       

32 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
- [Listing Form No. 40] through [Listing Form No. 60] shall be deleted.

These Enforcement Rules shall become effective on November 14, 2013. 

§2. Applicable Case Concerning Documents for Applying Initial Listing 

The amended provisions of [§12(2)11] shall apply starting with the company that submits the 
application for initial listing after the effective date of these Enforcement Rules.
