[Annex 3]Listing Fees and Annual Dues 

Listing Fees and Annual Dues 
(Pertaining to [§30]) 

1. Listing fees 

Initial listing, 
Supplementary 
listing 

Listing Fees 
The amounts calculated by multiplying market capitalization by following fee rates. 

Market capitalization 
(In KRW) 
≤  10 bil. 

>10 bil. and  ≤30 bil. 

>30 bil. and  ≤50 bil. 

>50 bil. and  ≤70 bil. 

>70 bil. and  ≤100 bil. 

>100 bil. and  ≤200 bil. 

>200 bil. and  ≤500 bil. 

>500 bil. 

Fee rates 

KRW 30,000 per KRW 1 bil. (Minimum KRW 50,000) 
KRW 300,000 + KRW 25,000 per KRW 1 billion for the 
market capitalization in excess of  KRW 10 billion 
KRW 800,000 + KRW 20,000 per KRW 1 billion for the 
market capitalization in excess of KRW 30 billion     
KRW 1.2 million + KRW 15,000 per KRW 1 billion for the 
market capitalization in excess of KRW 50 billion 
KRW 1.5 million + KRW 10,000 per KRW 1 billion for the 
market capitalization in excess of KRW 70 billion 
KRW 1.8 million + KRW 5,000 per KRW 1 billion for the 
market capitalization in excess of KRW 100 billion 
KRW 2.3 million + KRW 2,500 per KRW 1 billion for the 
market capitalization in excess of KRW 200 billion 
KRW 3.05 million + KRW 500 per KRW 1 billion for the 
market capitalization in excess of KRW 500 billion 
(Maximum amount: KRW 200 million) 

Listing change    KRW 500,000per case 

Notes:1. When determining the listing fees, the following market capitalization shall be used. 

Initial listing 

Supplementary 
listing 

Criteria for Fee Calculation 
Base market capitalization (The amount calculated by multiplying the number 
of listed stocks by the valuation price according to [Annex 1] of the 
Enforcement Rules of the KONEX Market Business Regulation as of the day 
immediately preceding the date of listing application) 
Market capitalization of new stocks to be listed (the amount determined by 
multiplying the number of new stocks to be listed by the closing price as of 
the day immediately preceding the date of listing application) 

2. The initial listing fees shall be imposed on the aggregate market capitalization amount of common 
stocks and different classes of stocks.   
3. The listing fees for supplementary listing shall be determined by application date, but the listing 
fees for supplementary listing by the exercise of warrants, conversion rights, and stock options shall 
be determined by the listing application date. 
4. The fees for supplementary listing shall be applied to the case of change of stock type resulting 
from the exercise of conversion rights. 
5. When determining the listing fees per KRW 1 billion of listing amount, the amount less than KRW 
1 billion shall be rounded up. 
6. In cases where an applicant for listing change submits several applications for listing change on 
a same day, listing change fees shall be determined by handling the applications filed on the same 
day as a single case. 

46 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
2. Annual Dues 

Annual Dues 
(Amounts less than KRW 100 shall be discarded) 

1. Annual dues paid regularly: On the basis of average total market capitalization of the 
previous year, the amount determined by applying the fee rate noted below. 

2. Annual dues paid irregularly: The amount determined by prorating, in proportion to the 
number of base days (the number of days from the first day to the day before the de-listing 
date of the year which includes the de-listing date) annual dues for the concerned year 
calculated by multiplying the rate shown in Table below to the average total market 
capitalization of the year up to the date of delisting decision.   

Average total market 
capitalization   
(In KRW billion) 
≤10 

>10 and  ≤30 

>30 and  ≤50 

>50 and  ≤70 

>70 and  ≤  100 

>100 and  ≤200 

>200 and  ≤500 

>500 

Fee Rates 

KRW 10,000 per KRW 1 billion 
KRW 100,000 + KRW 8,000 per KRW 1 billion of average total market 
capitalization in excess of KRW 10 billion   
KRW 260,000 + KRW 7,000 per KRW 1 billion of average total market 
capitalization in excess of KRW 30 billion 
KRW 400,000 + KRW 6,000 per KRW 1 billion of average total market 
capitalization in excess of KRW 50 billion 
KRW 520,000 + KRW 4,000 per KRW 1 billion of average total market 
capitalization in excess of KRW 70 billion 
KRW 640,000 + KRW 2,000 per KRW 1 billion of average total market 
capitalization in excess of KRW 100 billion 
KRW 840,000 + KRW 1,000 per KRW 1 billion of average total market 
capitalization in excess of KRW 200 billion 
KRW 1,140,000 + KRW 500 per KRW 1 billion of average total market 
capitalization in excess of KRW 500 billion 

Notes: 
1. When calculating the annual dues paid regularly, in the case of initial listing, it shall be the amount 
determined by prorating the amount calculated according to the method shown in Table  above in 
proportion to the number of days from the initial listing date to the last day of the concerned year. 
2. In the case of initial listing, the average total market capitalization shall be the average total market 
value of the concerned number of days. 
3.  The  average  total  market  capitalization  shall  be  determined  by  aggregating  the  market 
capitalizations of common stocks and class shares issued by the concerned listed corporation.   
4. When determining the fees per KRW 1 billion, the amount less than KRW 1 billion shall be rounded 
up.   
5. The average total market capitalization shall be determined by simple arithmetic average of the 
daily market capitalization. In such cases, if the trading is suspended, the market capitalization shall 
be calculated by multiplying the number of listed stocks by the base price.   

3. Payment Time of Listing Fees and Annual Dues 

47 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Payment Time 

Listing fees 

Regular payments 

Irregular payments 

The day immediately before listing 
For the stocks listed as of the end of last year, the annual dues for 
the last year shall be paid in January of each year. 
In case where stocks are delisted, the annual dues for the period 
from the first day of the year which includes the concerned 
delisting date to the previous day of delisting date shall be paid 
before the delisting date of the stocks concerned.   

4. Exemption from Payment of Listing Fees and Annual Dues 

The Exchange may exempt the listing fees and annual dues that fall under any of followings: 

(a)Listing fees and annual dues for listing change and supplementary listing of KONEX-listed 
corporations falling under [§28(2)4(c)] of the KONEX Market Listing Regulation; 

(b)Supplementary listing fees, listing change fees and annual dues of the stocks (including 
different  classes  of  stocks)  issued  by  the  KONEX-listed  corporations  who  are  under  the 
rehabilitation procedures pursuant to the Debtor Rehabilitation and Bankruptcy Act; 

(c) In case where a corporation is delisted during the period for regular payments or within 
three  (3)  months  after  the  payment  period  ended  (including  the  case  where  the  causes  for 
delisting  have  occurred,  while  excluding  the  case  of  being  delisted  after  the  improvement 
period was granted), the amount of annual dues for the period from the first day of the year 
which includes such delisting date to the previous day of the delisting date; or 

(d)In case where a corporation is delisted pursuant to [§28(1)5 and 6] (limited to the cases 
pursuant to Subparagraphs 5 and 6 of Article 227 of the Commercial Act) of the KONEX 
Market Listing Regulation, the amount of annual dues for the period from the first day of the 
year which includes the delisting date to the previous day of the delisting date. 

5. Other Matters relating to Listing Fees and Annual Dues 

(a)Notification of payment and measures against non-payment 

(i)  With  regard  to  the  payment  of  annual  dues,  the  Exchange  shall  notify  the  listed 
corporations  of  such  fact  by  the  day  two  (2)  weeks  before  the  due  date  for  the  regular 
payments and by the day one (1) week before the delisting date for the irregular payments.   

(ii) In cases where a listed corporation fails to pay the annual dues within three (3) months 
after the due date, the Exchange may file actions such as request for an order of payment 
against  the  concerned  corporation.  Provided  that,  this  provision  shall  not  apply  to  the 
delisted corporations. 

(b)Refund 

The Exchange shall refund the listing fees to the corporation of which listing application was 
rejected.

duties, etc.) shall be separately added and stated.

IV. Matters concerning Business 

74 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
1. Overview of business 

  A. Status and prospect of industry 

Note: 
1. In order to understand the overall industry to which the company belongs, describe matters such as industrial 
production trends, industrial characteristics, domestic and foreign market size trends, seasonal economic 
fluctuations, product lifecycles, alternative markets, resource procurement conditions, competition conditions, 
domestic and overseas regulatory conditions, and industry support policies, etc. If there are multiple business 
divisions, list each business division separately. 
2. Future prospects should be written based on objective data, and the source of the data should also be 
described. 

  B. Status of company 

Note: 
1. Describe in detail each period so that the business and production of the company from the time of 
establishment of the company to the application for listing can be easily understood. 
2. State specific motives and achievements for entering overseas markets, summary financial statements for the 
last three years of overseas branches and corporations, types of overseas expansion such as overseas local 
corporations, offices and equity investment, and joint ventures or alliance partners in the overseas countries, 
future plans, etc.   
3. Describe domestic and foreign competitors for major products and products, market share, etc. The market 
size, which is the basis of market share, is based on public data such as industry statistical data and industry 
journals. If such data is not available, the company's independent data or data collected by entrusting an external 
research agency may be used within the range of reliability, and the basis for calculating the market share shall 
be stated, but its rationality must be recognized. 
4. The existence and content of industry standards related to the production and sale of major products, etc., 
whether they were acquired, and the impact on the management of the company are described. 
5. Describe the details and prospects for new projects (new product development, new market development, 
etc.) that were newly promoted in the relevant business year in which the report submission date belongs, or that 
are newly implemented in the future through a resolution of the board of directors, etc. 

  C. Major business contracts 

Note: For the business management contract, trademark introduction contract, business license or franchise 
contract, and other major business contracts as of the date of submission of the report (including contracts that 
have not taken effect), enter the following items. However, if it is judged that the disclosure may cause 
significant loss as it falls under the company's trade secret, the details may be briefly described. 
a. contracting party 
b. Contract signing period and contract period 
c. Purpose and content of the contract 
d. Contract amount or payment method (standard), etc. 
e. Main contents of the contract

the matters specified in No. 1037.

5. Transactions with stakeholders, etc. 

Note: Describe transactions with the largest shareholder, etc., related parties and other interested parties in the 
following manner. 
1. The term “largest shareholder, etc.” includes the person under subparagraph 6 (a) of Article 2 of the Act on 
Governance of Financial Companies and a specially related person falling under any subparagraph of Article 3 
(1) of the Enforcement Decree of the Act.   
2. “Related parties” refers to related parties in Chapter 25 (Disclosure of Related Persons) of K-GAAP (K-IFRS 
No. 1024). 
3. “Other stakeholders” refers to those who are recognized as having an interest in the relevant company, such 
as transactions, bonds, and debt relationships with shareholders who own 10% or more of the stocks of the 
relevant company, excluding the largest shareholder. 
4. If the relevant company conducts transactions falling under “A” through “G” below with or for the 
stakeholders, etc. (including the case where the transaction is made in the account of the stakeholders, etc., 
regardless the name of transaction counterparty), describe the transaction details.

Guideline for Preparing Listing Eligibility Report 

I. Purpose 

The purpose of this guideline is to set out the necessary matters, such as the preparation method, 
content  and  scope  of  the  listing  eligibility  report,  which  a  designated  advisor  is  required  to 
submit to the Exchange in accordance with Article 12 (Application for Initial Listing) of the 
KONEX Market Listing Regulations. 

II. Definitions 

The terms used in this guideline and the notes in the form for the listing eligibility report shall 
be as follows. 

1. The term “report” refers to the listing eligibility report.   

2. The term “business year” refers to the accounting period stipulated in the articles of 
incorporation or related regulations of the company. 

3.The term “settlement date” and “semi-annual settlement date” refer to the end date of the 
business year and the date six months from the start date of the business year, respectively. 

4. The term “business division” is based on the subcategories of the Korean Standard Industrial 
Classification Table. However, if the management proposes a classification method that can 
properly reflect the diversification of business in consideration of the interrelationship between 
the economic activities of the enterprise, the profit-generating unit, the characteristics of the 
product and manufacturing process, and the characteristics of the market and sales method, it 
may be respected. 

5. The term “main place of business” means a unit of place or facility such as the head office, 
factory, branch, branch, or sales office, which is the basis for the performance of the purpose 
business such as production or sales activities of the enterprise. 

6. The term “products, etc.” refers to goods, products, services, and other objects of business 
that are ultimately produced as a result of the company's business activities. 

7. The term  “item” refers  to  products  or raw materials,  etc., which are classified by similar 
characteristics such as types or functions, but, if necessary, other classification methods shall 
be followed. 

8. The term “related parties” refers to related parties stipulated in Chapter 25 (Disclosure of 
Related Parties) of K-GAAP [No. 1024 (Disclosure of Related Parties) in K-IFRS (referring 
to Korean International Financial Reporting Standards)]. 

102 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
9. The term “related person” refers to a person who falls under any subparagraphs of Article 
3 (1) of the Enforcement Decree of the Financial Company Governance Act. 

10. The terms “corporate accounting standards” and “accounting auditing standards” refer to 
the accounting standards and audit standards set by the Financial Services Commission and the 
Korea Institute of Certified Public Accountants in accordance with Articles 5 and 16 of the Act 
on External Audit of Corporations, etc., respectively. 

11. The term “auditor” means the auditor under subparagraph 7 (a) of Article 2 of the Act on 
External Audit of Stock Companies, etc. 

12.  The  term  “auditor’s  audit  report”  refers  to  the  audit  report  stipulated  in  Accounting 
Standard 700 (Formulation of Opinion on Financial Statements and Reporting). 

13. Other terms used in this guideline shall be as stipulated in the Financial Investment Services 
and Capital Market Act and related regulations. In particular, the terms related to accounting 
and auditing follow as defined in the Corporate Accounting Standards and Auditing Standards. 

Ⅲ. General Principles 

1. Reports should be prepared based on objective data and facts, and expressions that may lead 
to misunderstanding or abstract or ambiguous terms should not be used. 

2. The contents of the report should be briefly and clearly described using terms that are easy 
to understand for easy understanding, but if deemed necessary to enhance understanding, they 
shall be prepared using diagrams, pictures, or photos. 

3. The report should be written in such a way that the details of the relevant company and the 
securities to be listed can be fully described. Therefore, all important matters should be stated, 
and the description of the contents that may cause adverse effects or unfavorable results for the 
company concerned shall not be omitted or missed. 

4. In principle, matters related to financial contents should be prepared for the last 3 business 
years  (including  the  half  year  of  the  relevant  business  year  if  the  half  year  of  the  relevant 
business year has passed) based on the adjusted financial statements on the audit report (if the 
financial statements for the half year of the relevant business year, the review report in cases 
of preparing the relevant review report or the financial statements confirmed by the designated 
advisor in cases of not preparing the review report) of auditor. However, if the settlement of 
accounts for the latest business year is not finalized, it shall be prepared for the last 3 business 
years immediately previous the latest business year and for the half year of the latest business 
year. 

5. Corporations subject to the preparation of consolidated financial statements shall prepare the 
report on the basis of individual (separate) financial statements, unless otherwise specified. 

IV. Base Time 

103 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
In  principle,  the  report  should  be  prepared  as  of  the  date  of  submission.  However,  stock 
distribution and financial matters may be prepared based on the settlement date or semi-annual 
settlement date to enhance the convenience in preparation and the comparability by period. 

V. Scope of Entry, etc. 

1. Scope of entry 

In relation to the preparation of the report, if the content to be included or method to enter in 
each part of the report is specified, the related contents or the non-applicable, in case of not 
relations, shall be stated. If the content or method is specified, matters deemed important in 
describing the company may be stated in an appropriate manner. 

2. Principle of materiality 

Whether or not specific facts or matters are material refers to matters deemed necessary for 
understanding the contents of the company, taking into consideration the Accounting Auditing 
Standards 320 (materiality in planning and conducting of audits). 

Ⅵ. Instructions for Filling out the Form, etc. 

1. In case where it is recognized that there is no risk of misunderstanding in consideration of 
the size of the company when entering the total amount of assets, sales amount, or sales quantity, 
etc., it may be omitted if it is less than one thousand or one million. However, this does not 
apply to matters related to (expected) public offering stocks. 

2. In the comparative presentation by business year, the latest business year is arranged on the 
right. 

3. “IV. Content of business” of the report shall be prepared according to the type of business 
such as manufacturing, construction, etc. 

VII. Submission of Report   

The  report  is  prepared  in  two  copies  and  submitted  together  with  the  storage  medium 
containing the report to the KONEX Market Department of the KOSDAQ Market Division of 
the Korea Exchange. 

104

106 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
[Listing Form No. 7] KONEX Market Listing Agreement 

KOSDAQ Market Listing Agreement for Domestic Companies 

We, the undersigned, (hereinafter referred to as “the Company”) enter into this Agreement with 
the Korea Exchange (hereinafter referred to as “the Exchange”) as per the following terms and 
conditions to list and trade the stocks issued by the Company on the KONEX market. 

Article 1. Observance of Laws and Regulations 

The Company shall observe faithfully the following laws and regulations, which are currently 
enforced, may be established, and amended from time to time in the future with respect to the 
operation of the KONEX market. 

1.  The Financial Investment Services and Capital Markets Act, the Enforcement Decree and 

the Enforcement Rules of the same Act and other related laws and regulations; 

2.  The  KONEX  Market  Listing  Regulation  and  the  Enforcement  Rules  of  the  same 

Regulation; 

3.  The  KONEX  Market  Business  Regulation  and  the  Enforcement  Rules  of  the  same 

Regulation; 

4.  The  KONEX  Market  Disclosure  Regulation  and  the  Enforcement  Rules  of  the  same 

Regulation; and 

5.  Other matters such as standards, guidelines and policies set forth by the Exchange or the 
parties that are authorized by the Exchange in relation to KONEX-listed corporations. 

Article 2. Cooperation with respect to Investigation of Abnormal Transactions 

In cases where the Exchange deems it necessary with respect to the investigation of abnormal 
transactions  of  listed  stocks,  it  may  request  the  Company,  in  writing  or  via  wired  and/or 
wireless communications, to submit copies of materials related to the process of creation of 
material corporate information (minutes of the board of directors, contracts etc.) including the 
time of generation of the information, list of executives and employees, personal information 
on  major  insiders,  list  of  shareholders,  etc.,  and  in  such  cases,  the  Company  shall  reply 
faithfully to the request. 

Article 3. Maintaining Corporate Continuity and Ensuring Management Transparency 

The  Company  shall  not  conduct  such  activities  as  unfair  fund  transactions  with  the  largest 

107 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
shareholder  and  the  related  persons  that  may  significantly  impede  maintaining  the 
independence  and  the  nature  as  a  going-concern  of  the  Company  and  shall  ensure  the 
transparency of management through refurbishing of articles of association and regulations, 
faithful performance of directors’ duties, transparent accounting practices, fair auditing, proper 
disclosure, prohibiting unfair inside transactions, protecting shareholders’ rights and interests, 
improving corporate governance, etc. 

Article 4. Measures 

In  cases  where  the  Exchange  deems  it  necessary  for  the  effective  implementation  of  this 
Agreement,  it  may  request  the  Company  for  necessary  matters,  in  writing  or  wired  and/or 
wireless communications, such as submission of related materials or reports, interviews with 
persons involved, etc., and in this case, the Company shall respond immediately to the request 
as long as there are no special reasons which are acknowledged by the Exchange. 

Article 5 Effect for successor 

This Agreement shall be effective for the person who succeeds the status of the Company or 
the Exchange. 

Article 6 Agreement on jurisdiction 

It is agreed upon that all disputes that may arise in relation to this Agreement shall be finally 
settled by the court with the jurisdiction over the location of the KONEX Market Division. 

Date:   

Name and signature/seal of the representative director: 

Name and signature/seal of the chairperson of KRX:

111 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
2. The definitions of terms used in the summary list of shareholders for the application for 
initial listing shall be as follows. 

 The largest shareholder refers to the person prescribed in [§2(6)] of the Regulation. 

The related person of the largest shareholder refers to the persons who have special 
relations with the largest shareholder (related persons in [§2(7)] of the Regulation, and the 
treasury stock refers to stocks owned by the corporation that is applying for initial listing. 

The major shareholder refers to a person falling under Subparagraph 6(b) of Article 2 of 
the Act on Corporate Governance of Financial Companies and defined as follows. In such 
cases, the “financial companies” shall be construed as “initial listing applicants”. However, 
the largest shareholder, his/her related persons and treasury stocks, institutional investors, and 
members of employee stock ownership association shall be excluded. 

The institutional investor refers to the person falling under the venture capital pursuant to 
[§2(5)] of the Regulation or the professional investors (person falling under any of each item 
of [§2(2)]) pursuant to [§2(6)] of the Regulation. However, the largest shareholder and 
his/her related persons and treasury stocks shall be excluded. 

The employee stock ownership association refers to the association established under 
Paragraph 4 of Article 2 of the Basic Workers Welfare Act. 

The minority shareholder refers to a person who holds less than 1/100 of total number of 
outstanding stocks. However, shareholders falling under item  through  shall be 
excluded. 

Other shareholders refer to shareholders who do not fall under any of through above.

4. Indicate the ratio to two decimal places. 

5. In the “Remarks” column, describe the relationship with the largest shareholder or the 
position in the company.

<Instructions for filling out the summary list of shareholders for the confirmation of 
stock distribution> 

114 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
1. The summary list of shareholders shall be prepared as of the end of the latest fiscal year (if 
the shareholder register is closed after the end of the latest business year, it shall be taken as of 
the closing date). Provided that, in cases where the corporation corresponds to the cause of the 
failure to meet the stock distribution criteria pursuant to [§24-2(2)1] and intends to prove the 
resolution of the cause, the summary list of shareholders shall be prepared based on the date of 
resolution of the cause. 

2. The definitions of terms  used in  the summary list  of shareholders for  the application  for 
initial listing shall be as follows. 

 The largest shareholder refers to the person prescribed in the main sentence of [§2(6)] of the 
Regulation, and the related person of the largest shareholder refers to the persons who have 
special relations with the largest shareholder (related persons in [§2(7)] of the Regulation). 

The treasury stock refers to stocks owned by the KONEX-listed corporation. 

The major shareholder refers to a person falling under Subparagraph 6(b) of Article 2 of the 
Act on Corporate Governance of Financial Companies. In such cases, the “financial companies” 
shall be construed as “KONEX-listed corporations”. However, the largest shareholder, his/her 
related  persons  and  treasury  stocks  and  the  employee  stock  ownership  association  shall  be 
excluded. 

 The institutional investor refers to the person falling under the venture capital pursuant to 
[§2(5)] of the Regulation or the professional investors (person falling under any of each item 
of [§2(2)]) pursuant to [§2(6)] of the Regulation, excluding the largest shareholder and related 
persons  and  treasury  stocks.  In  this  case,  the  institutional  investors  shall  be  classified  and 
described as “institutional investors who are major shareholders”, “minority shareholders”, and 
“other shareholders” according to their share ownership. 

The  employee  stock  ownership  association  refers  to  the  association  established  under 
Paragraph 4 of Article 2 of the Basic Workers Welfare Act. 

The minority shareholder refers to a person who holds less than 1/100 of total number of 
outstanding  stocks.  However,  the  largest  shareholder  and  related  persons,  treasury  stocks, 
major shareholders, and the employee stock ownership association shall be excluded. 

Other shareholders refer to shareholders who do not fall under the largest shareholders and 
related persons, treasury stocks, major shareholders, the employee stock ownership association, 
and minority shareholder. 

3. In table 1, the number of shareholders of the employee stock ownership association shall 
indicate the number of employees in the employee stock ownership association. 

4. In table 2 through 5, the shareholders with the largest number of common stocks are listed 
in order. 

5. Indicate the ratio to two decimal places.

6.  In  the  “Remarks”  column,  describe  the  relationship  with  the  largest  shareholder  or  the 
position in the company.

- Representative: 

- Corporation Registration Number: 

- Address: 

2. Relationship with Recommended Corporation   

3. Reason for Recommendation (Attached) 

Date:   
Name of recommending company: 
Name and seal of the representative director: 

118 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
<Instructions for Preparation> 

1.  “Recommended  corporation”  refers  to  the  corporation’s  articles  of  incorporation  and  a 
certified copy of corporate registration. 

2. “Relationship with recommended corporation” is written in consideration of the content and 
period of investment, guarantee, loan, etc. to the recommended corporation. 

3.  “Reason  for  recommendation”  shall  be  classified  in  terms  of  marketability,  investor 
protection, preparation for listing, etc. of the recommended corporation and stated in a separate 
attached document. 

a.  In  the  case  of  “marketability”,  industrial  growth  potential,  market  competition,  and  the 

possibility of changes in sales and profits are taken into consideration. 

b.  In  the  case  of  “investor  protection”,  the  disclosure  capacity  (whether  the  recommended 
corporation has a dedicated disclosure employee and whether the person has experience in 
disclosure work) and the ability to appoint a designated advisor (the ability to pay fees to 
the designated advisor of the recommended corporation and possibility of delisting due to 
non-appointment of designated advisors within one year after listing)). 

c. In the case of “preparation for listing”, whether the recommended corporation has undergone 
an  external  audit  [whether  the  recommended  corporation  receives  an  audit  opinion  of 
“unqualified”  for  the  entire  period  of  the  latest  business  year  or  the  first  half  of  the 
concerned  business  year,  and  whether  the  appointment  of  an  auditor  is  reported  to  the 
Securities  and  Futures  Commission  (Financial  Supervisory  Service)]  and  the  ability  to 
write an application for initial listing (ability to complete an application for initial listing 
review when a recommended corporation applies for initial listing), etc. are considered.

[Listing Form No. 21] Corporate Status Report 

Investors Note (Example) 

1. This report is a reference to the business management of the ABC Co. prepared by the 
XYZ company, a designated advisor to ABC Co. for the purpose of providing information 
for investors' investment judgment pursuant to Article 25 of the KONEX Market Listing 
Regulations  and  Article  21  of  the  same  Regulations.  Therefore,  investment  judgment 
should  not  be  made  solely  by  relying  on  the  matters  stated  in  this  report,  and  the 
responsibility for investment judgment belongs entirely to the investor. 

2. Please note that the forecast information in this report was prepared with due care based 
on the data submitted by ABC Co. by the time of writing this report, but it may differ 
from the actual results depending on the business situation and business environment of 
ABC Co. in the future. 

3. Please note that any damages caused by false entries and indications, or omissions or 
missing of important matters in this report are not subject to liability for compensation 
under  Article  125  of  the  Financial  Investment  Services  and  Capital  Markets  Act  and 
securities-related class action. 

133 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Investors Note (Example) 

※ For companies in the Startups Division or the Crowdfunding Corporation Division, 

please refer to the following information. 

1. This report is a reference prepared by the XYZ company on the matters related to its 
business management for the purpose of providing information for investors' investment 
judgment pursuant to Article 25 of the KONEX Market Listing Regulations and Article 
21 of the same Regulations. Therefore, investment judgment should not be made solely 
by  relying  on  the  matters  stated  in  this  report,  and  the  responsibility  for  investment 
judgment belongs entirely to the investor. 

2. Please note that the forecast information in this report was prepared with due care based 
on the data at the time of writing this report by ABC Co., but it may differ from the actual 
results depending on the business situation and business environment of ABC Co. in the 
future. 

3. Please note that any damages caused by false entries and indications, or omissions or 
missing of important matters in this report are not subject to liability for compensation 
under  Article  125  of  the  Financial  Investment  Services  and  Capital  Markets  Act  and 
securities-related class action.

III. Matters concerning Business 

1. Overview of business 

  A. Status and prospect of industry 

Note:   
1. In order to understand the overall industry to which the company belongs, describe matters such as industrial 
production trends, industrial characteristics, domestic and foreign market size trends, seasonal economic 
fluctuations, product lifecycles, alternative markets, resource procurement conditions, competition conditions, 
domestic and overseas regulatory conditions, and industry support policies, etc. If there are multiple business 
divisions, list each business division separately. 
2. Prospects should be written based on objective data, and the source of the data should also be described. 

  B. Status of company 

Note: 
1. Describe in detail each period so that the business and production of the company from the time of 
establishment of the company to the application for listing can be easily understood. 
2. State specific motives and achievements for entering overseas markets, summary financial statements for the 
last three years of overseas branches and corporations, types of overseas expansion such as overseas local 
corporations, offices and equity investment, and joint ventures or alliance partners in the overseas countries, 
plans, etc.   
3. Describe domestic and foreign competitors for major products and products, market share, etc. The market 
size, which is the basis of market share, is based on public data such as industry statistical data and industry 
journals. If such data is not available, the company's independent data or data collected by entrusting an external 
research agency may be used within the range of reliability, and the basis for calculating the market share shall 
be stated, but its rationality must be recognized. 
4. The existence and content of industry standards related to the production and sale of major products, etc., 
whether they were acquired, and the impact on the management of the company are described. 
5. Describe the details and prospects for new projects (new product development, new market development, 
etc.) that were newly promoted in the relevant business year in which the report submission date belongs, or that 
are newly implemented in the future through a resolution of the board of directors, etc. 

  C. Major business contracts 

Note: For the business management contract, trademark introduction contract, business license or franchise 
contract, and other major business contracts as of the date of submission of the report (including contracts that 
have not taken effect), enter the following items. However, if it is judged that the disclosure may cause

Ⅴ. Other Matters to Consider When Making Investment Decisions 

167 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Guideline for Preparing Corporate Status Report 

I. Purpose 

The purpose of this guideline is to set out the necessary matters, such as the preparation method, 
content and scope of the corporate status report, which a designated advisor (in the case of a 
corporation  in  the  Startups  Division  and  Crowdfunding  Corporation  Division,  the  relevant 
corporation) is required to submit to the Exchange in accordance with Article 25 (Corporate 
status report and disclosure) of the KONEX Market Listing Regulations. 

II. Definitions 

The terms used in these guidelines and the notes in the form for the corporate status report shall 
be as follows. 

1. The term “report” refers to the listing eligibility report.   

2. The term “business year” refers to the accounting period stipulated in the articles of 
incorporation or related regulations of the company. 

3. The term “settlement date” and “semi-annual settlement date” refer to the end date of the 
business year and the date six months from the start date of the business year, respectively. 

4. The term “business division” is based on the subcategories of the Korean Standard Industrial 
Classification Table. However, if the management proposes a classification method that can 
properly reflect the diversification of business in consideration of the interrelationship between 
the economic activities of the enterprise, the profit-generating unit, the characteristics of the 
product and manufacturing process, and the characteristics of the market and sales method, it 
may be respected. 

5. The term “main place of business” means a unit of place or facility such as the head office, 
factory, branch, branch, or sales office, which is the basis for the performance of the purpose 
business such as production or sales activities of the enterprise. 

6. The term “products, etc.” refers to goods, products, services, and other objects of business 
that are ultimately produced as a result of the company's business activities. 

7. The term  “item” refers  to  products  or raw materials,  etc., which are classified by similar 
characteristics such as types or functions, but, if necessary, other classification methods shall 
be followed. 

8. The term “related parties” refers to related parties stipulated in Chapter 25 (Disclosure of 
Related Parties) of K-GAAP [No. 1024 (Disclosure of Related Parties) in K-IFRS (referring 
to Korean International Financial Reporting Standards)]. 

9. The term “related person” refers to a person who falls under any subparagraphs of Article 
3 (1) of the Enforcement Decree of the Financial Company Governance Act. 

168 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
10. The terms “corporate accounting standards” and “accounting auditing standards” refer to 
the accounting standards and audit standards set by the Financial Services Commission and the 
Korea Institute of Certified Public Accountants in accordance with Articles 5 and 16 of the Act 
on External Audit of Corporations, etc., respectively. 

11. The term “auditor” means the auditor under subparagraph 7 (a) of Article 2 of the Act on 
External Audit of Stock Companies, etc. 

12.  The  term  “auditor’s  audit  report”  refers  to  the  audit  report  stipulated  in  Accounting 
Standard 700 (Formulation of Opinion on Financial Statements and Reporting). 

13. Other terms used in this guideline shall be as stipulated in the Financial Investment Services 
and Capital Market Act and related regulations. In particular, the terms related to accounting 
and auditing follow as defined in the Corporate Accounting Standards and Auditing Standards. 

Ⅲ. General Principles 

1. Reports should be prepared based on objective data and facts, and expressions that may lead 
to misunderstanding or abstract or ambiguous terms should not be used. 

2. The contents of the report should be briefly and clearly described using terms that are easy 
to understand for easy understanding, but if deemed necessary to enhance understanding, they 
shall be prepared using diagrams, pictures, or photos. 

3. The report should be written in such a way that the details of the relevant company and the 
securities to be listed can be fully described. Therefore, all important matters should be stated, 
and the description of the contents that may cause adverse effects or unfavorable results for the 
company concerned shall not be omitted or missed. 

4. In principle, matters related to financial contents should be prepared for the last two business 
years  and  the  period  of  the  1sthalfyear  of  the  relevant  business  year  based  on  the  adjusted 
financial statements on the audit report of auditor. However, if a separate period is specified in 
notes for each form, it shall be followed. 

5. Corporations subject to the preparation of consolidated financial statements shall prepare the 
report based on individual (separate) financial statements, unless otherwise specified. 

IV. Base Time 

In  principle,  the  report  should  be  prepared  as  of  the  date  of  submission.  However,  stock 
distribution and financial matters may be prepared based on the settlement date or semi-annual 
settlement date to enhance the convenience in preparation and the comparability by period. 

V. Scope of Entry, etc. 

169 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
1. Scope of entry 

In relation to the preparation of the report, if the content to be included or method to enter in 
each part of the report is specified, the related contents or the non-applicable, in case of not 
relations, shall be stated. If the content or method is specified, matters deemed important in 
describing the company may be stated in an appropriate manner. 

2. Principle of materiality 

Whether or not specific facts or matters are material refers to matters deemed necessary for 
understanding the contents of the company, taking into consideration the Accounting Auditing 
Standards 320 (materiality in planning and conducting of audits). 

Ⅵ. Instructions for Filling out the Form, etc. 

1. In case where it is recognized that there is no risk of misunderstanding in consideration of 
the size of the company when entering the total amount of assets, sales amount, or sales quantity, 
etc., it may be omitted if it is less than one thousand or one million. However, this does not 
apply to matters related to (expected) public offering stocks. 

2. In the comparative presentation by business year, the latest business year is arranged on the 
right. 

3. “IV. Content of business” of the report shall be prepared according to the type of business 
such as manufacturing, construction, etc. 

VII. Submission of Report   

The  report  is  prepared  in  two  copies  and  submitted  together  with  the  storage  medium 
containing the report to the KONEX Market Department of the KOSDAQ Market Division of 
the Korea Exchange.

Investors Note 

1. This application for initial listing examination was submitted to the Korea Exchange to 
apply for initial listing of ABC Company, and the listing approval of the Korea Exchange 
does not acknowledge that the statements in the application for initial listing examination 
are  true  or  accurate  and  not  guarantee  or  approve  the  value  of  the  stocks.  Therefore, 
investment  judgment  should  not  be  made  solely  by  relying  on  the  matters  stated  in  the 
application for initial listing examination, and the responsibility for investment judgment 
belongs entirely to the investor. 

2. Please note that the ABC Company prepared the financial information in this application 
for  initial  listing  examination  based  on  the  audit  report  of  XYZ  Company,  an  external 
auditor of ABC Company, prepared in accordance with the accounting standards of Article 
5(1)2 (or Subparagraph 1 of the same Article and same Paragraph) of the Act on External 
Audit of Stock Companies, etc. 

3. Please note that any damages caused by false entries and indications, or omissions of 
important matters in this listing eligibility report are not subject to liability for compensation 
under  Article  125  of  the  Financial  Investment  Services  and  Capital  Markets  Act  and 
securities-related class action. 

4.  Please  note  that  if  the  ABC  Company  does  not  enter  an  appointment  contract  for  a 
designated advisor by one year from the date of listing, it may be delisted in accordance 
with Article 28 (1) 12 of the KONEX Market Listing Regulations.

IV. Matters concerning Business 

1. Overview of business 

  A. Status and prospect of industry 

Note:   
1. In order to understand the overall industry to which the company belongs, describe matters such as industrial 
production trends, industrial characteristics, domestic and foreign market size trends, seasonal economic 
fluctuations, product lifecycles, alternative markets, resource procurement conditions, competition conditions, 
domestic and overseas regulatory conditions, and industry support policies, etc. If there are multiple business 
divisions, list each business division separately. 
2. Prospects should be written based on objective data, and the source of the data should also be described. 

  B. Status of company 

Note: 
1. Describe in detail each period so that the business and production of the company from the time of 
establishment of the company to the application for listing can be easily understood. 
2. State specific motives and achievements for entering overseas markets, summary financial statements for the 
last three years of overseas branches and corporations, types of overseas expansion such as overseas local 
corporations, offices and equity investment, and joint ventures or alliance partners in the overseas countries, 
plans, etc.   
3. Describe domestic and foreign competitors for major products and products, market share, etc. The market 
size, which is the basis of market share, is based on public data such as industry statistical data and industry 
journals. If such data is not available, the company's independent data or data collected by entrusting an external 
research agency may be used within the range of reliability, and the basis for calculating the market share shall 
be stated, but its rationality must be recognized. 
4. The existence and content of industry standards related to the production and sale of major products, etc., 
whether they were acquired, and the impact on the management of the company are described. 
5. Describe the details and prospects for new projects (new product development, new market development, 
etc.) that were newly promoted in the relevant business year in which the application submission date belongs, 
or that are newly implemented in the future through a resolution of the board of directors, etc. 

C. Major business contracts 

Note: For the business management contract, trademark introduction contract, business license or franchise 
contract, and other major business contracts as of the date of submission of the report (including contracts that 
have not taken effect), enter the following items. However, if it is judged that the disclosure may cause 
significant loss as it falls under the company's trade secret, the details may be briefly described. 
a. contracting party 
b. Contract signing period and contract period 
c. Purpose and content of the contract 
d. Contract amount or payment method (standard), etc. 
e. Main contents of the contract

4. Transaction details and other relationships with auditors (CPAs) 

Note: 
1. Enter the status of management consulting such as tax and accounting advice as well as the amount of 
payment. 
2. Write down whether the auditor (certified public accountant) has concurrently served as an outside director or 
an advisor, etc. of the relevant company. 
3. It should be prepared for the last 3 business years and the period up to the month immediately preceding the 
date of submission of the report. 

5. Matters concerning actions against accounting violations 

Note: Describe measures taken by the Securities and Futures Commission under Articles 26 (1) 3 and 26 (7) of 
the Regulations on External Audit and Accounting, etc. and the penalty surcharge imposed by Services 
Commission (Securities and Futures Commission) for the last 5 business years 

6. Tax audit, etc. 

Note: If the company has undergone a tax audit by the competent tax office, etc., or has been audited or 
inspected by a supervisory authority under relevant laws, etc. and has been pointed out for major errors in 
finance for the last five business years, state the contents and their impact on the financial statements.

business.

Guideline for Preparing Application for Initial Listing Examination 

I. Purpose 

The purpose of this guideline is to set out the necessary matters, such as the preparation method, 
content  and  scope  of  the  application  for  initial  listing  examination  which  a  technology 
evaluation corporation that intends to initially list its shares on the KONEX Market is required 
219 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
to submit to the Exchange in accordance with Article 13-2 (Special Cases for Initial Listing) 
of the KONEX Market Listing Regulations. 

II. Definitions 

The terms used in these guidelines and the notes in the form for the application for initial listing 
examination shall be as follows. 

1. The term “business year” refers to the accounting period stipulated in the articles of 
incorporation or related regulations of the company. 

2. The term “settlement date” and “semi-annual settlement date” refer to the end date of the 
business year and the date six months from the start date of the business year, respectively. 

3. The term “business division” is based on the subcategories of the Korean Standard Industrial 
Classification Table. However, if the management proposes a classification method that can 
properly reflect the diversification of business in consideration of the interrelationship between 
the economic activities of the enterprise, the profit-generating unit, the characteristics of the 
product and manufacturing process, and the characteristics of the market and sales method, it 
may be respected. 

4. The term “main place of business” means a unit of place or facility such as the head office, 
factory, branch, branch, or sales office, which is the basis for the performance of the purpose 
business such as production or sales activities of the enterprise. 

5. The term “products, etc.” refers to goods, products, services, and other objects of business 
that are ultimately produced as a result of the company's business activities. 

6. The term  “item” refers  to  products  or raw materials,  etc., which are classified by similar 
characteristics such as types or functions, but, if necessary, other classification methods shall 
be followed. 

7. The term “related parties” refers to related parties stipulated in Chapter 25 (Disclosure of 
Related Parties) of K-GAAP [No. 1024 (Disclosure of Related Parties) in K-IFRS (referring 
to Korean International Financial Reporting Standards)]. 

8. The term “related person” refers to a person who falls under any subparagraphs of Article 
3 (1) of the Enforcement Decree of the Financial Company Governance Act. 

9. The terms “corporate accounting standards” and “accounting auditing standards” refer to the 
accounting standards and audit standards set by the Financial Services Commission and the 
Korea Institute of Certified Public Accountants in accordance with Articles 5 and 16 of the Act 
on External Audit of Corporations, etc., respectively. 

10. The term “auditor” means the auditor under subparagraph 7 (a) of Article 2 of the Act on 
External Audit of Stock Companies, etc. 

11.  The  term  “auditor’s  audit  report”  refers  to  the  audit  report  stipulated  in  Accounting 
220 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Standard 700 (Formulation of Opinion on Financial Statements and Reporting). 

12. Other terms used in this guideline shall be as stipulated in the Financial Investment Services 
and Capital Market Act and related regulations. In particular, the terms related to accounting 
and auditing follow as defined in the Corporate Accounting Standards and Auditing Standards. 

Ⅲ. General Principles 

1. The application for initial listing examination should be prepared based on objective data 
and facts, and expressions that may lead to misunderstanding or abstract or ambiguous terms 
should not be used. 

2. The contents of the application for initial listing examination should be briefly and clearly 
described  using  terms  that  are  easy  to  understand  for  easy  understanding,  but  if  deemed 
necessary to enhance understanding, they shall be prepared using diagrams, pictures, or photos. 

3. The application for initial listing examination should be written in such a way that the details 
of the relevant company and the securities to be listed can be fully described. Therefore, all 
important matters should be stated, and the description of the contents that may cause adverse 
effects or unfavorable results for the company concerned shall not be omitted or missed. 

4. In principle, matters related to financial contents should be prepared for the last 3 business 
years  (including  the  half  year  of  the  relevant  business  year  if  the  half  year  of  the  relevant 
business year has passed) based on the adjusted financial statements on the audit report (if the 
financial statements for the half year of the relevant business year, the review report in cases 
of preparing the relevant review report or the financial statements confirmed by the designated 
advisor in cases of not preparing the review report) of auditor. However, if the settlement of 
accounts for the latest business year is not finalized, it shall be prepared for the last 3 business 
years immediately previous the latest business year and for the half year of the latest business 
year. 

5. Corporations subject to the preparation of consolidated financial statements shall prepare the 
report based on individual (separate) financial statements, unless otherwise specified. 

IV. Base Time 

In principle, the application for initial listing examination should be prepared as of the date of 
submission. However, stock distribution and financial matters may be prepared based on the 
settlement date or semi-annual settlement date to enhance the convenience in preparation and 
the comparability by period. 

V. Scope of Entry, etc. 

1. Scope of entry 

In relation to the preparation of the application for initial listing examination, if the content to 
221 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
be included or method to enter in each part of the report is specified, the related contents or 
the non-applicable, in case of not relations, shall be stated. If the content or method is 
specified, matters deemed important in describing the company may be stated in an 
appropriate manner. 

2. Principle of materiality 

Whether or not specific facts or matters are material refers to matters deemed necessary for 
understanding the contents of the company, taking into consideration the Accounting Auditing 
Standards 320 (materiality in planning and conducting of audits). 

Ⅵ. Instructions for Filling out the Form, etc. 

1. In case where it is recognized that there is no risk of misunderstanding in consideration of 
the size of the company when entering the total amount of assets, sales amount, or sales quantity, 
etc., it may be omitted if it is less than one thousand or one million. However, this does not 
apply to matters related to (expected) public offering stocks. 

2. In the comparative presentation by business year, the latest business year is arranged on the 
right. 

3. “IV. Content of business” of the report shall be prepared according to the type of business 
such as manufacturing, construction, etc. 

VII. Submission of the Application for Initial Listing Examination 

The application for initial listing examination is prepared in two copies and submitted together 
with  the  storage  medium  containing  the  report  to  the  KONEX  Market  Department  of  the 
KOSDAQ Market Division of the Korea Exchange. 

[Listing Form No. 22-1] Application for Initial Listing Examination for Crowdfunding 
Corporation 
[August 4, 2017] (Amended on March 20, 2019; April 17, 2019; September 10, 2019; June 10, 2020) 

Investors Note 

1. This application for initial listing examination was submitted to the Korea Exchange to 
apply for initial listing of ABC Company, and the listing approval of the Korea Exchange 
does not acknowledge that the statements in the application for initial listing examination 
are  true  or  accurate  and  not  guarantee  or  approve  the  value  of  the  stocks.  Therefore, 
investment  judgment  should  not  be  made  solely  by  relying  on  the  matters  stated  in  the 
application for initial listing examination, and the responsibility for investment judgment 
222 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
belongs entirely to the investor. 

2. Please note that the ABC Company prepared the financial information in this application 
for  initial  listing  examination  based  on  the  audit  report  of  XYZ  Company,  an  external 
auditor of ABC Company, prepared in accordance with the accounting standards of Article 
5(1)2 (or Subparagraph 1 of the same Article and same Paragraph) of the Act on External 
Audit of Stock Companies, etc. 

3. Please note that any damages caused by false entries and indications, or omissions of 
important matters in this listing eligibility report are not subject to liability for compensation 
under  Article  125  of  the  Financial  Investment  Services  and  Capital  Markets  Act  and 
securities-related class action. 

4.  Please  note  that  if  the  ABC  Company  does  not  enter  an  appointment  contract  for  a 
designated advisor by one year from the date of listing, it may be delisted in accordance 
with Article 28 (1) 13 of the KONEX Market Listing Regulations.

To the Korea Exchange, 

We, the undersigned, herewith provide this confirmation letter in relation with the listing 
examination carried out by the Korea Exchange to verify the listing eligibility based on the 
application for initial listing examination submitted by the ____ Company 

-  There are no omissions of statements or indications of material facts or false statements 
or misrepresentation in the materials in the application for initial listing examination. 
-  The financial statements and financial matters included in the  application for initial 
listing examination are consistent with those audited or reviewed by the auditor. 
-  The ____ Company has legal ownership of all assets, and no collateral or mortgage is 
established  for  any  of  the  _____  Company's  assets  except  for  matters  listed  in  the 
application for initial listing examination. 

-  The  Company  has  stated  all  actual  liabilities,  contingent  liabilities,  and  guarantees 

provided to the third parties in the application for initial listing examination. 

If the above-mentioned matters are found to be different from the facts, we will bear all 
civil and criminal liabilities arising from them, and we promise not to raise any objection 
to any measures taken by the Korea Exchange.

4. In the title of the position, it should be written in detail such as director, outside director, auditor, outside auditor, 
advisor, consultant, commissioned, etc., and whether full-time or registered is indicated in parentheses 
5. Relations with the largest shareholder and the CEO are described. 
6. In the remarks, the previous career and period should be written in the case of new appointment, re-
appointment and promotion, and the new workplace and position in case of retirement, and concurrent positions, 
if any, are included.

Note: State whether the stocks, etc. issued by the company are electronically registered in accordance with 
Articles 25 through 27 of the Act on Electronic Registration of Stocks and Bonds.

Note: If there is a fact that the company or the CEO has been disciplined or sanctioned for violating various 
laws or obligations such as finance-related laws and tax laws (including tax investigations) within the last 5 
business years, the date, reason, and details shall be entered.

equity ratio of 10% or more during the last 3 business years, the name of the company, the amount invested and 
the share ownership ratio, the amount, the reason and the date of default and normalization (plan) of the 
bankruptcy are additionally described.

IV. Matters concerning Business 

1. Overview of business 

  A. Status and prospect of industry 

Note:   
1. In order to understand the overall industry to which the company belongs, describe matters such as industrial 
production trends, industrial characteristics, domestic and foreign market size trends, seasonal economic 
fluctuations, product lifecycles, alternative markets, resource procurement conditions, competition conditions, 
domestic and overseas regulatory conditions, and industry support policies, etc. If there are multiple business 
divisions, list each business division separately. 
2. Prospects should be written based on objective data, and the source of the data should also be described. 

  B. Status of company 

Note: 
1. Describe in detail each period so that the business and production of the company from the time of 

244 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
establishment of the company to the application for listing can be easily understood. 
2. State specific motives and achievements for entering overseas markets, summary financial statements for the 
last three years of overseas branches and corporations, types of overseas expansion such as overseas local 
corporations, offices and equity investment, and joint ventures or alliance partners in the overseas countries, 
plans, etc.   
3. Describe domestic and foreign competitors for major products and products, market share, etc. The market 
size, which is the basis of market share, is based on public data such as industry statistical data and industry 
journals. If such data is not available, the company's independent data or data collected by entrusting an external 
research agency may be used within the range of reliability, and the basis for calculating the market share shall 
be stated, but its rationality must be recognized. 
4. The existence and content of industry standards related to the production and sale of major products, etc., 
whether they were acquired, and the impact on the management of the company are described. 
5. Describe the details and prospects for new projects (new product development, new market development, 
etc.) that were newly promoted in the relevant business year in which the application submission date belongs, 
or that are newly implemented in the future through a resolution of the board of directors, etc. 

C. Major business contracts 

Note: For the business management contract, trademark introduction contract, business license or franchise 
contract, and other major business contracts as of the date of submission of the report (including contracts that 
have not taken effect), enter the following items. However, if it is judged that the disclosure may cause 
significant loss as it falls under the company's trade secret, the details may be briefly described. 
a. contracting party 
b. Contract signing period and contract period 
c. Purpose and content of the contract 
d. Contract amount or payment method (standard), etc. 
e. Main contents of the contract

of the relevant company.

3) A company in which the persons prescribed in 1) or 2) directly or indirectly influence the management or 

business.

5. Transactions with stakeholders, etc. 

Note: Describe transactions with the largest shareholder, etc., related parties and other interested parties in the 
following manner.

Governance of Financial Companies and a specially related person falling under any subparagraph of Article 3 
(1) of the Enforcement Decree of the Act.   
2. “Related parties” refers to related parties in Chapter 25 (Disclosure of Related Persons) of K-GAAP (K-IFRS 
No. 1024). 
3. “Other stakeholders” refers to those who are recognized as having an interest in the relevant company, such 
as transactions, bonds, and debt relationships with shareholders who own 10% or more of the stocks of the 
relevant company, excluding the largest shareholder.

  C. Use of funds 

Note: 
1. In the case of facility investment funds, describe in detail the outline of the facility investment (name of the 
project, production scale, etc.), investment period, total investment amount, amount and method of previous 
funding, and amount and method to be raised in the future. 
2. In the case of operating funds, specify the customer (or creditor), the time of use, the amount and details of 
use. 
3. The public offering amount shall be the lowest among the range of the expected public offering price to be 
presented at the time of book building and indicate that the usage of the funds (deposits are not considered as 
use of public offering funds) is 90% or more of the public offering amount. 
4. State the funds that can be raised additionally according to the over-allocation option separately, and if the 
purpose of the funds is different from the original purpose of the public offering, specify it. 

4. Calculation method of public offering (private placement) price 

Note: Describe in detail the method of calculating the public offering (private placement) price. 

271 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Guideline for Preparing Application for Initial Listing Examination 

I. Purpose 

The purpose of this guideline is to set out the necessary matters, such as the preparation method, 
content  and  scope  of  the  application  for  initial  listing  examination  which  a  technology 
evaluation corporation that intends to initially list its shares on the KONEX Market is required 
to submit to the Exchange in accordance with Article 13-2 (Special Cases for Initial Listing) 
of the KONEX Market Listing Regulations. 

II. Definitions 

The terms used in these guidelines and the notes in the form for the application for initial listing 
examination shall be as follows. 

1. The term “business year” refers to the accounting period stipulated in the articles of 
incorporation or related regulations of the company. 

2. The term “settlement date” and “semi-annual settlement date” refer to the end date of the 
business year and the date six months from the start date of the business year, respectively. 

3. The term “business division” is based on the subcategories of the Korean Standard Industrial 
Classification Table. However, if the management proposes a classification method that can 
properly reflect the diversification of business in consideration of the interrelationship between 
the economic activities of the enterprise, the profit-generating unit, the characteristics of the 
product and manufacturing process, and the characteristics of the market and sales method, it 
may be respected. 

4. The term “main place of business” means a unit of place or facility such as the head office, 
factory, branch, branch, or sales office, which is the basis for the performance of the purpose 
business such as production or sales activities of the enterprise. 

5. The term “products, etc.” refers to goods, products, services, and other objects of business 
that are ultimately produced as a result of the company's business activities. 

6. The term  “item” refers  to  products  or raw materials,  etc., which are classified by similar 
characteristics such as types or functions, but, if necessary, other classification methods shall 
be followed. 

7. The term “related parties” refers to related parties stipulated in Chapter 25 (Disclosure of 
Related Parties) of K-GAAP [No. 1024 (Disclosure of Related Parties) in K-IFRS (referring 
to Korean International Financial Reporting Standards)]. 

8. The term “related person” refers to a person who falls under any subparagraphs of Article 
3 (1) of the Enforcement Decree of the Financial Company Governance Act. 

9. The terms “corporate accounting standards” and “accounting auditing standards” refer to the 
272 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
accounting standards and audit standards set by the Financial Services Commission and the 
Korea Institute of Certified Public Accountants in accordance with Articles 5 and 16 of the Act 
on External Audit of Corporations, etc., respectively. 

10. The term “auditor” means the auditor under subparagraph 7 (a) of Article 2 of the Act on 
External Audit of Stock Companies, etc. 

11.  The  term  “auditor’s  audit  report”  refers  to  the  audit  report  stipulated  in  Accounting 
Standard 700 (Formulation of Opinion on Financial Statements and Reporting). 

12. Other terms used in this guideline shall be as stipulated in the Financial Investment Services 
and Capital Market Act and related regulations. In particular, the terms related to accounting 
and auditing follow as defined in the Corporate Accounting Standards and Auditing Standards. 

Ⅲ. General Principles 

1. The application for initial listing examination should be prepared based on objective data 
and facts, and expressions that may lead to misunderstanding or abstract or ambiguous terms 
should not be used. 

2. The contents of the application for initial listing examination should be briefly and clearly 
described  using  terms  that  are  easy  to  understand  for  easy  understanding,  but  if  deemed 
necessary to enhance understanding, they shall be prepared using diagrams, pictures, or photos. 

3. The application for initial listing examination should be written in such a way that the details 
of the relevant company and the securities to be listed can be fully described. Therefore, all 
important matters should be stated, and the description of the contents that may cause adverse 
effects or unfavorable results for the company concerned shall not be omitted or missed. 

4. In principle, matters related to financial contents should be prepared for the last 3 business 
years  (including  the  half  year  of  the  relevant  business  year  if  the  half  year  of  the  relevant 
business year has passed) based on the adjusted financial statements on the audit report (if the 
financial statements for the half year of the relevant business year, the review report in cases 
of preparing the relevant review report or the financial statements confirmed by the designated 
advisor in cases of not preparing the review report) of auditor. However, if the settlement of 
accounts for the latest business year is not finalized, it shall be prepared for the last 3 business 
years immediately previous the latest business year and for the half year of the latest business 
year. 

5. Corporations subject to the preparation of consolidated financial statements shall prepare the 
report based on individual (separate) financial statements, unless otherwise specified. 

IV. Base Time 

In principle, the application for initial listing examination should be prepared as of the date of 
submission. However, stock distribution and financial matters may be prepared based on the 
settlement date or semi-annual settlement date to enhance the convenience in preparation and 
the comparability by period. 

273 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
V. Scope of Entry, etc. 

1. Scope of entry 

In relation to the preparation of the application for initial listing examination, if the content to 
be included or method to enter in each part of the report is specified, the related contents or 
the non-applicable, in case of not relations, shall be stated. If the content or method is 
specified, matters deemed important in describing the company may be stated in an 
appropriate manner. 

2. Principle of materiality 

Whether or not specific facts or matters are material refers to matters deemed necessary for 
understanding the contents of the company, taking into consideration the Accounting Auditing 
Standards 320 (materiality in planning and conducting of audits). 

Ⅵ. Instructions for Filling out the Form, etc. 

1. In case where it is recognized that there is no risk of misunderstanding in consideration of 
the size of the company when entering the total amount of assets, sales amount, or sales quantity, 
etc., it may be omitted if it is less than one thousand or one million. However, this does not 
apply to matters related to (expected) public offering stocks. 

2. In the comparative presentation by business year, the latest business year is arranged on the 
right. 

3. “IV. Content of business” of the report shall be prepared according to the type of business 
such as manufacturing, construction, etc. 

VII. Submission of the Application for Initial Listing Examination 

The application for initial listing examination is prepared in two copies and submitted together 
with  the  storage  medium  containing  the  report  to  the  KONEX  Market  Department  of  the 
KOSDAQ Market Division of the Korea Exchange.

party undersigned.

the party undersigned, as the person subject to mandatory holding of stocks, etc., violate relevant 
regulations by presale contract, etc.; and not to raise any objection to any measures to be taken by 
the Exchange.
